mrun /ds/production/medhistory/apache2/i386-linux-thread-multi/bin/apache_restart.sh -- ds16 ds17 ds18 ds19 ds20 ds21

#build_al_index
#!/usr/bin/perl

# al_index_manager: Audit Log Index Manager
# This is a command-line interface to the BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr modules
#
# Author: jmh
#
# Version history:
# 1/10/2006 - Initial release
# 6/4/2007  - Added completion email capability
# 2/2/2016  - Added 'prune_al_index' capability to clean down indexes by retention period 

use warnings;
use strict;

use Data::Dumper;
use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use Mail::SendEasy;

our $VERSION = '1.1';
our $TEMP_DIR = $ENV{TMPDIR};	# temp files for building indexes will go here

our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
our $SMTP_SERVER = $ENV{DEFAULT_SMTP_SERVER};

die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

initialize_logging(logfile => "$DS_BASE_DIR/common/log/al_index_mgr.$$.log", screen_only => 0, screen_threshold => 'ERROR', file_threshold => 'ERROR');

my %params_date_spec_required = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Mandatory range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 0
	}
);

my %params_date_spec_optional = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Optional range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 1
	}
);

my %params_index_spec_required = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 0 } );
my %params_index_spec_optional = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );
my %params_connection_var = ( connection_var => { description => 'Name of environment variable for database connection', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_agg_buckets_optional = ( agg_buckets => { description => 'Number of work units to spread aggregation phase over (e.g. 10, 20, 35, etc)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '35' } );

#my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

#my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_build_priority_spec = ( build_priority => { description => "CPU scheduling priority (nice value from 0 to 19)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '19' } );

#my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx:2' } );
my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_index_profile_attributes = (
                description         =>  { description => 'Description of index (duh)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                field_id            =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP field id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                segment_id          =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP segment id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_function  =>  { description => 'Name of BLUELITE::Normalize function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_params    =>  { description => 'Parameters for normalize_function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                valid_only_ind      =>  { description => "Set to 1 to limit indexing to 'valid' values when using normalize_function", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                hash_method         =>  { description => "Name of BLUELITE::Normalize hash_method to apply (e.g. 'crc16')", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_begin  =>  { description => 'First process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_end    =>  { description => 'Last process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1}
);

our $script_name = $0;
$script_name =~ s|.*/||g;	# get basename

our $command_meta = {

	build_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index (unconditional)',

		param_validation => {
			%params_date_spec_required,
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&build_al_index
	},

	create_al_index => {
		description => 'Define profile for new index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&create_al_index
	},

	drop_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove all index data and profile',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&drop_al_index
	},

	enable_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index only on process dates not yet enabled',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&enable_al_index
	},

	remove_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove index data',	

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&remove_al_index
	},
	
	update_al_index => {
		description => 'Update profile for existing index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&update_al_index
	},
	
	prune_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove expired process dates for existing indexes',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
		},

		method => \&prune_al_index
	},
};


sub general_usage() {

	print "$script_name version $VERSION\n";
	print "Usage:                         $script_name -email addresses -command -command_parameters\n";
	print "Alternate (equivalent) usage:  command -command_parameters\n\n";
	print "Supported commands are:\n\n";

	foreach my $command (keys %{$command_meta}) {
		print "$command	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{description} . "\n";
	}

	print "\nTo get command-specific help use '$script_name -command -help'  or  'command -help'\n";
}

sub command_usage($) {
  my $command = shift;

	print "Usage: $command -parameters\n";
	print "\nRequired parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && (! $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "\nOptional parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if ((! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) ||
			(exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})
		) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "	-email	Comma-seperated list of email addresses to send to upon completion\n";
}


my $command;

if (! exists($command_meta->{$script_name})) {
	$command = lc(shift @ARGV);
	$command =~ s/^--?//;

	if (($command =~ /^-?-?help/i) or ($command eq '')) {
		general_usage;
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! exists($command_meta->{$command})) {
		die "ERROR: Command '$command' is not supported by the index manager\n";
	}
} else {
	$command = $script_name;
}

if (! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation})) {
	die "ERROR: Command '$command' has no 'param_validation' info in source code!\n";
}

if ((! defined($ARGV[0])) or ($ARGV[0] =~ /^-?-?help/i)) {
	command_usage($command);
	exit(1);
}

my %option = validate_with (
	params  => \@ARGV,
	spec    => {
							%{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}},
							email => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 }
							},
	called  => $command,
	normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^--?//; return uc $k }
);


our @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS = ();
if (exists($option{CONNECTION_VAR})) {
	push(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS, connection_var => $option{CONNECTION_VAR});
	delete $option{CONNECTION_VAR};
}

#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;

our $index_mgr = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr->new(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

if (! defined($index_mgr)) {
	die "ERROR: Unable to get new object from BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr\n";
}

##############################################

sub create_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->new_index_profile(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create new index profile object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($index_profile->save_index_profile));

	return 1;
}


sub prune_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  
	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, uc($option->{INDEX_ID}))) {
				
    my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);
    
	  if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
	  	die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object for index : '$index_id'\n";
	  }
		
	  return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));
	  print "\n";
	}
	
	return 1;
}


sub update_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  my $parallel_hosts;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not load existing index profile object\n";
	}

	if (defined($option{PARALLEL_HOSTS})) {
		$parallel_hosts = $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
		delete $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
	}

	$index_profile->save_index_profile(%{$option});

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (defined($parallel_hosts)) {
		$maint_grp->parallel_hosts($parallel_hosts);
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));

	return 1;
}


sub index_ids_to_objects($) {
  my $index_ids = shift;
  my %index_list;

	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, $index_ids)) {

		$index_list{$index_id} = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

		if (! defined($index_list{$index_id})) {
			die "ERROR: Could not obtain index object for index_id '$index_id'\n";
		}

	}

	return %index_list;
}


sub convert_process_dates($) {
  my $options = shift;
  my (%process_dates);

	if (defined($options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
		foreach my $element (split(/[,\s]+/, $options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
			if ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				$process_dates{$1} = 1;

			} elsif ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*-\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				if (! exists($options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN})) {
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN} = $1;
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_END} = $2;
				} else {
					die "ERROR: Currently, only 1 process date range may be specified\n";
				}

			} else {
				die "ERROR: process date spec of '$element' is not valid\n";
			}
		}

		if (scalar(keys %process_dates) >= 1) {
			@{$options->{PROCESS_DATES}} = (sort keys %process_dates);
		}

		delete $options->{PROCESS_DATE};
	}

	return $options;
}


sub build_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->rebuild));

	return 1;
}


sub enable_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, temp_dir => $TEMP_DIR, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	# get a list of all defined indexes if none specified on command line

	if (! exists($option->{INDEX_ID})) {
		foreach my $index_id ($index_mgr->all_indexes) {
			$maint_grp->add_index($index_id);
		}
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->enable));

	return 1;
}


sub remove_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return $maint_grp->delete;
}


sub drop_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
	my %indexes = index_ids_to_objects($option->{INDEX_ID});
  my $undeleted_profiles = 0;
#print "HEY\n";
#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;
  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (! $maint_grp->delete) {
		return undef;
	}

	foreach my $index_id (keys %indexes) {

		if (! $indexes{$index_id}->delete_index_profile) {

			print STDERR "ERROR: All index data deleted for index '$index_id', but unable to remove it's index profile definition from database\n";
			$undeleted_profiles++;
		}
	}

	if ($undeleted_profiles) {
		return undef;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}


sub email(@) {

  my $mail = new Mail::SendEasy( smtp => $SMTP_SERVER);

  if (! defined($mail) ) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to establish a SMTP connection to $SMTP_SERVER\n";
    return undef;
  }

  my $status = $mail->send(
    from => 'data.services@relayhealth.com',
    from_title => 'RelayHealth Data Services',
    @_
  );

  if (! $status) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Failed to be send email\n";
    return undef;
  }

  return 1;
}


##############################################

my ($exit_status, $email);

if (defined($option{EMAIL})) {
	$email = $option{EMAIL};
	delete $option{EMAIL};
}

if ((exists($command_meta->{$command}->{method})) && (exists(&{$command_meta->{$command}->{method}}))) {
	my $ret;

	eval { $ret = $command_meta->{$command}->{method}(\%option) };

	warn $@ if $@;

  my $completion_status;

	if (! defined($ret)) {
		$exit_status = 1;
		$completion_status = 'failed';
	} else {
		$exit_status = 0;
		$completion_status = 'succeeded';
	}

	if (defined($email)) {

		my $option_list = Dumper(\%option);
		$option_list =~ s/\$VAR1/options/;

		email(
			to => $email,
			subject => "$command process $completion_status",
			msg => "The following $command process ${completion_status}:\n\n$option_list\n" . join("\n", $@) . "\n"
		);
	}

	exit($exit_status);
} else {
	die "ERROR: Interface for '$command' not yet supported\n";
}



#build_encrypt
#!/usr/bin/perl

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
#
# build_encrypt
#
# command line utility to create an encrypted database connection string
# for use by versions of Build.pm that support it.
#
# 20150605 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# taking code from filed_encrypt
#
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

package DS::Build;

use strict;
use warnings;
use Crypt::Simple;
use IO::File;

STDOUT->autoflush(1);
STDERR->autoflush(1);

# turn off local echo
system('stty -echo');

my $pw1 = '';
my $pw2 = '';
while ( !$pw1 ) {

	# prompt for password
	print "Enter the password .............. : ";
	chomp( $pw1 = <STDIN> );
	print "\n";

	if ( !$pw1 ) {
		print "The password cannot be blank.\n";
		next;
	}

	# verify passwd
	while ( !$pw2 ) {

		# prompt for password a second time
		print "Enter the password again ........ : ";
		chomp( $pw2 = <STDIN> );
		print "\n";

	}

	if ( $pw1 ne $pw2 ) {
		print "Passwords don't match - please try again\n";
		$pw1 = '';
		$pw2 = '';
	}

} ## end while ( !$pw1 )

# enable local echo
system('stty echo');

my $encrypted = encrypt($pw1);

print "Encrypted password is ........... :\n\n", $encrypted, "\n\n";
print "Build config connect string is .. :\n\n";
print "<username>/{$encrypted}\@dbi:Oracle:<DSDEV|DSQA|DSPROD>\n\n";

exit(0);

#c1_to_c2
#!/usr/bin/perl

our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

$lookup_dir = "$DS_BASE_DIR/common/etc";	# default lookup dir

$zip_population_file_basename = 'zip_population.dat';
$restricted_provider_zip_population_file_basename = 'restricted_prov_zip_population.dat';

$prog_name = $0;

use Getopt::Std;

if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
	if (-t 0) {
		print STDERR "Usage: $prog_name [-c] [-p 2|23|full] [-r restricted_provider_zip_file] [-z zip_population_file] [-d reference_dir] [input_file]\n";
		exit(1);
	}
}

getopts('cp:r:z:d:');

if (defined($opt_c)) {
	$compress_output = 1;
} else {
	$compress_output = 0;
}

if (defined($opt_d)) {
	$lookup_dir = $opt_d;
}

# jmh, 20041202, fixed 2 assignments below, as they were previously transposed
$zip_population_file = "$lookup_dir/$zip_population_file_basename";
$restricted_provider_zip_population_file = "$lookup_dir/$restricted_provider_zip_population_file_basename";

# Initialize restricted provider zipsec info

if (defined($opt_r)) {
	$restricted_provider_zip_population_file = $opt_r;
}

if (defined($opt_z)) {
	$zip_population_file = $opt_z;
}

$restricted_provider_zip_method = '2';

if (defined($opt_p)) {
	if ($opt_p eq '23') {
		$restricted_provider_zip_method = '23';
		open(RESTR_PROV_ZIP, $restricted_provider_zip_population_file) || die "Cannot open restricted provider zip population file $restricted_provider_zip_population_file : $!\n";
		while (<RESTR_PROV_ZIP>) {
			chomp;
			$line = $_;

			# ignore comment or blank lines
			if ($line =~ /^\s*#|^\s*$/) {
				next;
			}

			if ($line =~ /^\s*([0-9][0-9][0-9])\s*$/) {
				$RESTRICTED_PROVIDER_ZIPSEC{$1} = 1;
			} else {
				die "ERROR: Invalid zipsec listed in restricted provider zip population file $restricted_provider_zip_population_file ($line)\n";
			}
		}
	} elsif ($opt_p eq '2') {
		$restricted_provider_zip_method = '2';
	} elsif ($opt_p eq 'full') {
		$restricted_provider_zip_method = 'full';
	} else {
		die "ERROR: '$opt_p' is not a valid restricted provider zip method for -p option\n";
	}
}

sub replace_substr() {
  my($in_val) = shift;
  my($start_pos) = shift;
  my($end_pos) = shift;
  my($replace_val) = shift;
  my($begin_val, $end_val, $formatted_substr, $input_length);

	# make position values 0-based instead of 1-based
	$start_pos--;
	$end_pos--;

	$input_length = length($in_val);

	if ($start_pos > 0) {
		$begin_val = substr($in_val, 0, $start_pos);
	}

	if ($end_pos + 1 <= $input_length) {
		$end_val = substr($in_val, $end_pos + 1);
	}

	$field_length = $end_pos - $start_pos + 1;

	if ($start_pos + $field_length > $input_length) {
		$field_length = $input_length - $start_pos;
	}

	$formatted_substr = sprintf("%-${field_length}.${field_length}s", $replace_val);

	return $begin_val . $formatted_substr . $end_val;
}

sub range_substr() {
	my($input_val) = shift;
	my($start_pos) = shift;
	my($end_pos) = shift;

	return substr($input_val, $start_pos - 1, $end_pos - $start_pos + 1);
}

foreach $rec_type (@VALID_RECORD_TYPES) {
	$VALID_REC_TYPES{$rec_type} = 1;
}

# load low-population zips

if (! -f $zip_population_file) {
	die "ERROR: Unable to find $zip_population_file file\n";
}

open(ZIP_POP, $zip_population_file) || die "ERROR: Unable to open $zip_population_file file : $!\n";

while (<ZIP_POP>) {

	chomp;
	$zip = $_;

	$FACILITY_LOW_POPULATION{$zip} = 1;

}

close(ZIP_POP);

if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
	if (-t 0) {
		print STDERR "$prog_name: ERROR: Standard input cannot be a terminal when input_file is not specified\
n";
		exit(1);
	} else {
		$INPUT = *STDIN;
	}
} else {
	$input_files = join(' ', @ARGV);

	if (! open(IN, "read_file $input_files |")) {
		print STDERR "$prog_name: ERROR: Unable to start uncompressing input files $input_files : $!\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$INPUT = *IN;
}

if ($compress_output) {
	if (! open($OUTPUT, "| gzip -c")) {
		print STDERR "$prog_name: ERROR: Unable to start compressing output for $input_files : $!\n";
		exit(1);
	}
} else {
	$OUTPUT = *STDOUT;
}

while (<$INPUT>) {
  chomp;
  $input_rec = $_;
  $output_rec = $_;

  $rec_type3 = substr($input_rec, 0, 3);
  $rec_type2 = substr($input_rec, 0, 2);

  if ((! defined($VALID_REC_TYPES{$rec_type3}) and (! defined($VALID_REC_TYPES{$rec_type2})))) {
		next;	# skip invalid records
  }

  SWITCH: {

	# NSF records

	/^[ABCXYZ]A0/	&& do {
		# reset "current claim" variables since this record necessarily means we are no longer processing the previous claim
		$source_of_pay = '';
	};

	/^[ABYZ]A0/	&& do {
		# reset "current batch" variables since this record necessarily means we are no longer processing the previous batch
		$prov_tax_id = '';
	};

	/^BA0/	&& do {

			$prov_tax_id = &range_substr($output_rec, 32, 40);

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^BA1/	&& do {

			# change provider zips to 2 digits for Tulsa restricted accounts (tax id is blank or all 0)

			if ($prov_tax_id =~ /^[ 0]*$/) {	
				$provider_zip1 = &range_substr($output_rec, 117, 125);
				$provider_zip2 = &range_substr($output_rec, 218, 226);
				$provider_zip1 =~ s/^ +//;
				$provider_zip1 =~ s/ +$//;
				$provider_zip2 =~ s/^ +//;
				$provider_zip2 =~ s/ +$//;

                                if ($restricted_provider_zip_method eq '2') {

                                        # 2 digit method
					$provider_zip1 = substr($provider_zip1, 0, 2);
					$provider_zip2 = substr($provider_zip2, 0, 2);

                                } elsif ($restricted_provider_zip_method eq '23') {

                                        # 2 or 3 digit method

					$provider_zipsec1 = substr($provider_zip1, 0, 3);

                                        if (defined($RESTRICTED_PROVIDER_ZIPSEC{$provider_zipsec1})) {
						$provider_zip1 = substr($provider_zip1, 0, 2);
                                        } else {
						$provider_zip1 = $provider_zipsec1;
                                        }

					$provider_zipsec2 = substr($provider_zip2, 0, 3);

                                        if (defined($RESTRICTED_PROVIDER_ZIPSEC{$provider_zipsec2})) {
						$provider_zip2 = substr($provider_zip2, 0, 2);
                                        } else {
						$provider_zip2 = $provider_zipsec2;
                                        }
                                } elsif ($restricted_provider_zip_method ne 'full') {
                                        die "ERROR: Don't know what provider zip to use because restricted_provider_zip_method variable is set to an invalid value of '$restricted_provider_zip_method'\n";
				}

				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 117, 125, $provider_zip1);
				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 218, 226, $provider_zip2);
			}

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^DA0/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 69, 88);	# group no
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 89, 121);	# group name
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 214, 214);	# insured MI
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 215, 217);	# insured generation

			$source_of_pay = &range_substr($output_rec, 24, 24);

			if ($source_of_pay =~ /^[Aa0]$/) {	# if self pay
				$output_rec =&replace_substr($output_rec, 36, 68);	# payer name
			}

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^DA1/	&& do {
			if ($source_of_pay =~ /^[Aa0]$/) {	# if self pay
				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 23, 52);	# payer addr 1
				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 53, 82);	# payer addr 2
				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 83, 102);	# payer city
				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 105, 113);	# payer zip
			}

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^DA2/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 124, 131);	# insured retire date
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 132, 139);	# insured spouse retire 
			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^EA0/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 32, 33);	# accident/symptom date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 52, 53);	# release of info date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 61, 62);	# same/similar symptom date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 70, 71);	# disability from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 78, 79);	# disability to date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 161, 162);	# admission date1 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 169, 170);	# discharge date1 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 207, 208);	# prov signature date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 273, 274);	# date last seen DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 281, 282);	# date document sent DD

			last SWITCH;
	};


	/^EA1/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 167, 168);	# return to work date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 175, 176);	# consult/surgery date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 183, 184);	# admission date2 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 191, 192);	# discharge date2 DD

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 258, 277);	# emt/paramedic last name
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 278, 289);	# emt/paramedic first name
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 290, 290);	# emt/paramedic middle name

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^EA7/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 117, 148);	# facility/lab zip code encrypted
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 149, 180);	# facility/lab zipsec1 encrypted
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 181, 183);	# facility/lab zipsec2

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^FA0/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 46, 47);	# service from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 54, 55);	# service to date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 219, 220);	# serum creatine date DD

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 207, 209);	# patient weight

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^FB0/	&& do {
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 149, 150);	# prescription date DD

			$hpsa_facility_zip = &range_substr($output_rec, 173, 181);
			$hpsa_facility_zip =~ s/^ +//;
			$hpsa_facility_zipsec = substr($hpsa_facility_zip, 0, 3);

			# 3 digit zipsec or 2 digit zipsec, based on population

			if (defined($FACILITY_LOW_POPULATION{$hpsa_facility_zipsec})) {
				$zipsec = substr($hpsa_facility_zip, 0, 2);
			} else {
				$zipsec = substr($hpsa_facility_zip, 0, 3);
			}

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 173, 181, $zipsec);

			last SWITCH;
	};

	# UB records

	/^01/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 161, 162);	# processing date DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^10/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 80, 81);	# NDC processing date DD

			$prov_tax_id = &range_substr($output_rec, 8, 17);

			# change provider zips to 2 or 3 digits for Tulsa restricted accounts (tax id is blank or all 0)

			if ($prov_tax_id =~ /^[ 0]*$/) {
				$provider_zip = &range_substr($output_rec, 163, 171);
				$provider_zip =~ s/^ +//;
				$provider_zip =~ s/ +$//;

				if ($restricted_provider_zip_method eq '2') {

					# 2 digit method
					$provider_zip = substr($provider_zip, 0, 2);

				} elsif ($restricted_provider_zip_method eq '23') {

					# 2 or 3 digit method

					$provider_zipsec = substr($provider_zip, 0, 3);

					if (defined($RESTRICTED_PROVIDER_ZIPSEC{$provider_zipsec})) {
						$provider_zip = substr($provider_zip, 0, 2);
					} else {
						$provider_zip = $provider_zipsec;
					}
                                } elsif ($restricted_provider_zip_method ne 'full') {
                                        die "ERROR: Don't know what provider zip to use because restricted_provider_zip_method variable is set to an invalid value of '$restricted_provider_zip_method'\n";
				}

				$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 163, 171, $provider_zip);
			}

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^20/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 289, 290);	# admission date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 299, 300);	# statement covers from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 307, 308);	# statement covers through date DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^30/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 169, 185);	# group number
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 186, 199);	# group name

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^34/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 141, 142);	# authorization from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 149, 150);	# authorization thru date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 232, 233);	# authorization from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 240, 241);	# authorization thru date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 323, 324);	# authorization from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 331, 332);	# authorization thru date DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^40/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 272, 273);	# occurrence date 1 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 282, 283);	# occurrence date 2 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 292, 293);	# occurrence date 3 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 302, 303);	# occurrence date 4 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 312, 313);	# occurrence date 5 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 322, 323);	# occurrence date 6 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 332, 333);	# occurrence date 7 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 342, 343);	# occurrence span from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 350, 351);	# occurrence span through date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 360, 361);	# occurrence span from date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 368, 369);	# occurrence span through date DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^60/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 120, 121);	# service date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 176, 177);	# service date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 232, 233);	# service date DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^61/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 122, 123);	# revenue date of service DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 178, 179);	# revenue date of service DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 234, 235);	# revenue date of service DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

	/^70/	&& do {

			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 136, 137);	# principle procedure date DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 151, 152);	# other procedure date 1 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 166, 167);	# other procedure date 2 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 181, 182);	# other procedure date 3 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 196, 197);	# other procedure date 4 DD
			$output_rec = &replace_substr($output_rec, 211, 212);	# other procedure date 5 DD

			last SWITCH;
	};

  }

  print $OUTPUT $output_rec . "\n" || die "Unable to write record to output: $!\n";

}

if (! close($OUTPUT)) {
	print STDERR "$prog_name: ERROR: Problem closing or writing compressed output for $input_files: $!\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (! close($INPUT)) {
	print STDERR "$prog_name: ERROR: Problem closing or reading compressed input files $input_files: $!\n";
	exit(1);
}



#c1_to_c2_wrap
#!/usr/bin/perl

use Getopt::Std;

$PGM = $0;
$EXIT_SUCCESS = 0;

if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
	print "Usage: $PGM -d output_dir | -t output_dir_top -h dest_host [-c] [-r modtime_ref_file] input_file
	-c	Do not generate c2 if it already exists and is newer than input_file
	-r	Set modification time of generated c2 file to be same as modtime_ref_file\n";
}

getopts('d:t:h:cdr:');

if (defined($opt_r)) {
	$modtime_ref_file = $opt_r;

	if (! -f $modtime_ref_file) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Mod time reference file $modtime_ref_file does not exist!\n";
		exit(1);
	}
}

if (defined($opt_d)) {
	$DEBUG = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_c)) {
	$skip_if_newer = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_h)) {
	$host = $opt_h;
} else {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Must specify remote_host via -h option\n";
	exit(1);
}

$input_file = $ARGV[0];

if (length($input_file) == 0) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: No input file specified!\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (system("ls $input_file > /dev/null 2>&1") != 0) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Input file $input_file does not exist!\n";
	exit(1);
}

$input_file_basename = $input_file;
$input_file_basename =~ s|^.*/([^/]+)$|$1|;

if ($input_file_basename =~ /^(NSF|UB)e_([A-Z]+)_([0-9]+)(.*)$/i) {
	($type, $source, $date, $suffix) = ($1, $2, $3, $4);
	$output_file_basename = "${type}e2_${source}_${date}${suffix}";
} else {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Cannot construct output file name from input file name $input_file\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (defined($opt_d)) {
	$output_dir = $opt_d;
} elsif (defined($opt_t)) {
	$output_dir_top = $opt_t;

	$month = substr($date, 0, 6);

	if (length($month) != 6) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: determine month for input file $input_file\n";
		exit(1);
	}


	$output_dir = "${output_dir_top}/${month}";

	#if ( (! -d $output_dir) && (! -l $output_dir)) {
	#	system('mkdir', $output_dir);
	#}
}

if ( (! -d $output_dir) && (! -l $output_dir) ) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: The output directory $output_dir does not exist!\n";
	exit(1);
}

sub my_exit() {

	if ((-f $output_file) and (-f $modtime_ref_file)) {
		system('touch', '-c', '-r', $modtime_ref_file, $output_file);
	}

	exit($_[0]);
}

$output_file = "$output_dir/$output_file_basename";

if (-f $output_file) {
	if ($skip_if_newer) {
		($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$file_size,$atime,$outfile_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($output_file);
		($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$file_size,$atime,$inputfile_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($input_file);

		if ($outfile_mtime >= $inputfile_mtime) {
			if ($DEBUG) {
				print STDERR "debug: existing output file $output_file is newer or same age as input file $input_file . Skipping c2 generation\n";
			}

			exit($EXIT_SUCCESS);
		} else {
			print STDERR "Regenerating older existing c2 file $output_file\n";
		}
	} else {
		if ($DEBUG) {
			print STDERR "debug: existing file $output_file will be overwritten\n";
		}
	}
} else {
	if ($DEBUG) {
		print STDERR "debug: new c2 file will be generated: $output_file\n";
	}
}

if (! open(C2, "c1_to_c2 -c $input_file |")) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to start c1_to_c2 process on input file $input_file: $!\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (! open(OUT, "> $output_file")) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to create output file $output_file for input file $input_file: $!\n";
	exit(1);
}

while (<C2>) {
	if (! print OUT $_) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to write line to $output_file for input file $input_file: $!\n";
		&my_exit(1);
	}
}


if (! close(C2)) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to close or read from c1_to_c2 process on input file $input_file: $!\n";
	&my_exit(1);
}

if (! close(OUT)) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to close output file $output_file for input file $input_file: $!\n";
	&my_exit(1);
}

print STDERR "c2 file generated: $output_file\n";

&my_exit($EXIT_SUCCESS);


#chartex
#!/usr/bin/perl -w

eval 'exec /usr/bin/perl -w
 -S $0 ${1+"$@"}'
    if 0; # not running under some shell

#######################################################################
#
# chartex - A utility to extract charts from an Excel file for
# insertion into a Spreadsheet::WriteExcel file.
#
# reverse('©'), September 2007, John McNamara, jmcnamara@cpan.org
#
# Documentation after __END__
#


use strict;
use OLE::Storage_Lite;
use Getopt::Long;
use Pod::Usage;


my $man         = 0;
my $help        = 0;
my $in_chart    = 0;
my $chart_name  = 'chart';
my $chart_index = 1;
my $sheet_index = -1;
my @sheetnames;
my @exrefs;
my $depth_count = 0;
my $max_font    = 0;

#
# Do the Getopt and Pod::Usage routines.
#
GetOptions(
            'help|?'    => \$help,
            'man'       => \$man,
            'chart=s'   => \$chart_name,
          ) or pod2usage(2);

pod2usage(1) if $help;
pod2usage(-verbose => 2) if $man;


# From the Pod::Usage pod:
# If no arguments were given, then allow STDIN to be used only
# if it's not connected to a terminal (otherwise print usage)
pod2usage() if @ARGV == 0 && -t STDIN;




# Check that the file can be opened because OLE::Storage_Lite won't tell us.
# Possible race condition here. Could fix with latest OLE::Storage_Lite. TODO.
#
my $file = $ARGV[0];

open  TMP, $file or die "Couldn't open $file. $!\n";
close TMP;

my $ole      = OLE::Storage_Lite->new($file);
my $book97   = pack 'v*', unpack 'C*', 'Workbook';
my $workbook = ($ole->getPpsSearch([$book97], 1, 1))[0];

die "Couldn't find Excel97 data in file $file.\n" unless $workbook;


# Write the data to a file so that we can access it with read().
my $tmpfile = IO::File->new_tmpfile();
binmode $tmpfile;

my $biff = $workbook->{Data};
print {$tmpfile} $biff;
seek $tmpfile, 0, 0;



my $header;
my $data;

# Read the file record by record and look for a chart BOF record.
#
while (read $tmpfile, $header, 4) {

    my ($record, $length) = unpack "vv", $header;
    next unless $record;

    read $tmpfile, $data, $length;

    # BOUNDSHEET
    if ($record == 0x0085) {
        push @sheetnames, substr $data, 8;
    }

    # EXTERNSHEET
    if ($record == 0x0017) {
        my $count = unpack 'v', $data;

        for my $i (1 .. $count) {
            my @tmp = unpack 'vvv', substr($data, 2 +6*($i-1));
            push @exrefs, [@tmp];
        }

    }

    # BOF
    if ($record == 0x0809) {
        my $type = unpack 'xx v', $data;

        if ($type == 0x0020) {
            my $filename = sprintf "%s%02d.bin", $chart_name, $chart_index;
            open    CHART, ">$filename" or die "Couldn't open $filename: $!";
            binmode CHART;

            my $sheet_name = $sheetnames[$sheet_index];
            $sheet_name .= ' embedded' if $depth_count;

            printf "\nExtracting \%s\ to %s", $sheet_name, $filename;
            $in_chart = 1;
            $chart_index++;
        }
        $depth_count++;
    }


    # FBI, Chart fonts
    if ($record == 0x1060) {

        my $index = substr $data, 8, 2, '';
           $index = unpack 'v', $index;

        # Ignore the inbuilt fonts.
        if ($index >= 5) {
            $max_font = $index if $index > $max_font;

            # Shift index past S::WE fonts
            $index += 2;
        }

        $data .= pack 'v', $index;
    }

    # FONTX, Chart fonts
    if ($record == 0x1026) {

        my $index = unpack 'v', $data;

        # Ignore the inbuilt fonts.
        if ($index >= 5) {
            $max_font = $index if $index > $max_font;

            # Shift index past S::WE fonts
            $index += 2;
        }

        $data = pack 'v', $index;
    }



    if ($in_chart) {
        print CHART $header, $data;
    }


    # EOF
    if ($record == 0x000A) {
            $in_chart = 0;
            $depth_count--;
            $sheet_index++ if $depth_count == 0;
;
    }
}


if ($chart_index > 1) {
    print "\n\n";
    print "Add the following near the start of your program\n";
    print "and change the variable names if required.\n\n";
}
else {
    print "\nNo charts found in workbook\n";
}

for my $aref (@exrefs) {
    my $sheet1 = $sheetnames[$aref->[1]];
    my $sheet2 = $sheetnames[$aref->[2]];

    my $range;

    if ($sheet1 ne $sheet2) {
        $range = $sheet1 . ":" .  $sheet2;
    }
    else {
        $range = $sheet1;
    }

    $range = "'$range'" if $range =~ /[^\w:]/;

    print "    \$worksheet->store_formula('=$range!A1');\n";
}

print "\n";

for my $i (5 .. $max_font) {

    printf "    my \$chart_font_%d = \$workbook->add_format(font_only => 1);\n",
                $i -4;

}





__END__


=head1 NAME

chartex - A utility to extract charts from an Excel file for insertion into a Spreadsheet::WriteExcel file.

=head1 DESCRIPTION

This program is used for extracting one or more charts from an Excel file in binary format. The charts can then be included in a C<Spreadsheet::WriteExcel> file.

See the C<add_chart_ext()> section of the  Spreadsheet::WriteExcel documentation for more details.


=head1 SYNOPSIS

chartex [--chartname --help --man] file.xls

    Options:
        --chartname -c  The root name for the extracted charts,
                        defaults to "chart".


=head1 OPTIONS

=over 4

=item B<--chartname or -c>

This sets the root name for the extracted charts, defaults to "chart". For example:

    $ chartex file.xls

    Extracting "Chart1" to chart01.bin


    $ chartex -c mychart file.xls

    Extracting "Chart1" to mychart01.bin

=item B<--help or -h>

Print a brief help message and exits.


=item B<--man or -m>

Prints the manual page and exits.

=back


=head1 AUTHOR

John McNamara jmcnamara@cpan.org


=head1 VERSION

Version 0.02.


=head1 COPYRIGHT

© MMV, John McNamara.

All Rights Reserved. This program is free software. It may be used, redistributed and/or modified under the same terms as Perl itself.

#checkzip.sh

status=0

for f in $*
  do
	case $f in
	*.zip)	cmd=unzip
		;;
	*.gz)	cmd=gunzip
		;;
	*)	echo "cannot determine file type"
		exit 1
		;;
	esac

	$cmd -t $f > /dev/null 2>&1
	if [ "$?" -ne 0 ]
	  then
		echo "$f:ERROR"
		status=1
	  else
		echo "$f:OK"
	fi
  done

exit $status


#check_CAData.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl

# ===============================================================
#  _____  ___   ______      _                 _                               
# /  __ \/ _ \  |  _  \    | |               | |                              
# | /  \/ /_\ \ | | | |__ _| |_ __ _ ___  ___| |_                             
# | |   |  _  | | | | / _` | __/ _` / __|/ _ \ __|                            
# | \__/\ | | | | |/ / (_| | || (_| \__ \  __/ |_                             
#  \____|_| |_/ |___/ \__,_|\__\__,_|___/\___|\__|
#
#  _____           _            _____ _               _    
# |  ___|         (_)          /  __ \ |             | |   
# | |____  ___ __  _ _ __ ___  | /  \/ |__   ___  ___| | __
# |  __\ \/ / '_ \| | '__/ _ \ | |   | '_ \ / _ \/ __| |/ /
# | |___>  <| |_) | | | |  __/ | \__/\ | | |  __/ (__|   < 
# \____/_/\_\ .__/|_|_|  \___|  \____/_| |_|\___|\___|_|\_\
#           |_|                                            
#                                                                    
# check_CAData.pl
# ===============================================================
# Author : Isaac Lim (eg8gpb7)
# VerDate: v1.0 / 28SEP2015
# CorrectAddress Dataset Expiration Check
# ===============================================================


# for dev use only
#use lib ('/ds/development/QASL3/dev/common/lib');

use DateTime;
use Date::Calc qw/Delta_Days/;
use Data::Dumper;
use DS::QASL;
use Getopt::Long;
use BLUELITE::Common qw(email);
use DS::DSLOG;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;


sub Usage() {
  print "\n---------------------------------------\n";
  print "CorrectAddress Dataset Expiration Check :: $PGM\n";
  print "---------------------------------------\n";
  print "Usage 1: $PGM -env <dev|qaqc|prod>\n\n";
  print "Option:\n";
  print "  -email <email_list>\n\n";
  print "note: email list option is comma separated and is required in order to send emails\n";
}

my ($email_list,$env);

if (! @ARGV) {
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

my $ret = GetOptions(
  'email=s' => \$email_list,
  'env=s' => \$env,
);

if (! $ret) {
  print "\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if (! $env) {
  die "Environment type (dev/qaqc/prod) required. please provide -env option.\n";
} elsif (lc $env =~ /^(dev|qaqc|prod)$/) {
  $ENV{LOG_ENV_NAME} = $ENV{ENV_NAME} = $env;
} else {
  die "Could not recognize -env option \"$env\". Use dev/qaqc/prod...\n";
}

#if (! $email_list) {
#  die "Unable to retrieve email list. Not emailing out!";
#}

my $DSLOG = DS::DSLOG->new(
  APP_ID => 'DSMONITOR',
  PROCESS => 'CA_DATA_CHECK',
  LOG_LEVEL => 'INFO',
  MESSAGE => 'Starting Check'
);


my $build_dt;
my ($year, $month, $day);

my $qas_object = DS::QASL->new();
my $build_date = $qas_object->get_build_date()->{BuildDate};

if ($build_date =~ /^\s*(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2})\s*$/) {
  ($year, $month, $day) = ($1, $2, $3);
  $build_dt = DateTime->new(year => $year, month => $month, day => $day);
} else {
  die "Build date not in YYYYMMDD format\n";
}

my $today = DateTime->today();
my $expire_dt = $build_dt->clone->add(days => 105);
my $ninety_day_check_dt = $build_dt->clone->add(days => 90);

my @today_arr = ($today->year, $today->month, $today->day);
my @expire_date_arr = ($expire_dt->year, $expire_dt->month, $expire_dt->day);
my $dd = Delta_Days(@today_arr, @expire_date_arr);

my $cmp = DateTime->compare($today, $ninety_day_check_dt);

my $msg;
if ($cmp >= 0) {
  if ( $dd < 0 ) {
    # RED -- EXPIRED!
    $msg = "CA Data is expired! Address validation will not work.";
    $DSLOG->log(EVENT_CODE => 'ERROR', LOG_LEVEL => 'FATAL', MESSAGE => $msg);
  } elsif ( $dd <= 10 ) {
    # RED
    $msg = "CA Data will expire on $expire_date_arr[0]$expire_date_arr[1]$expire_date_arr[2]!";
    $DSLOG->log(EVENT_CODE => 'ERROR', LOG_LEVEL => 'FATAL', MESSAGE => $msg);
  } else {
    # YELLOW
    $msg = "90 days has passed and new CA Data has not been loaded yet. Please check for new dataset...";
    $DSLOG->log(EVENT_CODE => 'WARN', LOG_LEVEL => 'WARN', MESSAGE => $msg);
  }
  if ($email_list && $msg) {
    BLUELITE::Common::email(
    to => $email_list,
    subject => "CorrectAddress Data Expiration (generated from $env)",
    message => $msg,
    );
  }
} else {
  $DSLOG->log(EVENT_CODE => 'OK', LOG_LEVEL => 'INFO', MESSAGE => 'CorrectAddress Data is OK');
}


#check_CAWS.sh
#!/bin/bash

# ===============================================================
#    ___  _     __    __     _     __
#   / __\/_\   / / /\ \ \___| |__ / _\_   _____
#  / /  //_\\  \ \/  \/ / _ \ '_ \\ \\ \ / / __|
# / /__/  _  \  \  /\  /  __/ |_) |\ \\ V / (__
# \____|_/ \_/   \/  \/ \___|_.__/\__/ \_/ \___|
#
#                     _ _               __    __           _             
#   /\/\   ___  _ __ (_) |_ ___  _ __  / / /\ \ \___  _ __| | _____ _ __ 
#  /    \ / _ \| '_ \| | __/ _ \| '__| \ \/  \/ / _ \| '__| |/ / _ \ '__|
# / /\/\ \ (_) | | | | | || (_) | |     \  /\  / (_) | |  |   <  __/ |   
# \/    \/\___/|_| |_|_|\__\___/|_|      \/  \/ \___/|_|  |_|\_\___|_|   
#
#                                                                       
# check_CAWS.sh 
# ===============================================================
# Author : Isaac Lim (eg8gpb7)
# VerDate: v1.0 / 15SEP2015
# Correct Address WebService Monitor Worker
# ===============================================================

# ===============================================================
#                      Variable Declarations
# ===============================================================

CA1_PROTO="http"
CA1_HOST="dsgrid01b.ndchealth.com"
CA1_PORT="13080"
CA1_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA1_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

CA2_PROTO="http"
CA2_HOST="dsgrid02b.ndchealth.com"
CA2_PORT="13080"
CA2_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA2_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

CA3_PROTO="http"
CA3_HOST="dsgrid03b.ndchealth.com"
CA3_PORT="13080"
CA3_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA3_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

CA4_PROTO="http"
CA4_HOST="dsgrid04b.ndchealth.com"
CA4_PORT="13080"
CA4_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA4_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

CA5_PROTO="http"
CA5_HOST="dsgrid05b.ndchealth.com"
CA5_PORT="13080"
CA5_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA5_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

CA6_PROTO="http"
CA6_HOST="dsgrid06b.ndchealth.com"
CA6_PORT="13080"
CA6_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
CA6_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

LB_PROTO="http"
LB_HOST="dsgrid02a.ndchealth.com"
LB_PORT="13080"
LB_CONTEXT="CorrectAddressWS"
LB_URL="wsStatus.jsp"

source .bash_profile 1> /dev/null 2>&1


Usage() {
  echo "CorrectAddress WebService Monitor - invalid target/option \"${1}\""
  echo "Usage:  $0  CA1|CA2|CA3|CA4|CA5|CA6|LB  [-s]"
  echo "  CA1 - (node1) dsgrid01b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  CA2 - (node2) dsgrid02b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  CA3 - (node3) dsgrid03b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  CA4 - (node4) dsgrid04b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  CA5 - (node5) dsgrid05b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  CA6 - (node6) dsgrid06b.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  LB  - (loadbalancer) dsgrid02a.ndchealth.com:13080/CorrectAddressWS/wsStatus.jsp"
  echo "  -s  - silent mode"
}

# Parse the command parameters
if [ "A${1}" == "A" ]
then
  Usage ${1}
  exit 6
elif [ "${1}" == "CA1" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA1_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA1_HOST}
  PORT=${CA1_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA1_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA1_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "CA2" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA2_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA2_HOST}
  PORT=${CA2_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA2_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA2_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "CA3" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA3_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA3_HOST}
  PORT=${CA3_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA3_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA3_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "CA4" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA4_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA4_HOST}
  PORT=${CA4_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA4_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA4_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "CA5" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA5_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA5_HOST}
  PORT=${CA5_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA5_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA5_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "CA6" ]
then
  PROTO=${CA6_PROTO}
  HOST=${CA6_HOST}
  PORT=${CA6_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${CA6_CONTEXT}
  URL=${CA6_URL}
elif [ "${1}" == "LB" ]
then
  PROTO=${LB_PROTO}
  HOST=${LB_HOST}
  PORT=${LB_PORT}
  CONTEXT=${LB_CONTEXT}
  URL=${LB_URL}
else
  Usage ${1}
  exit 6
fi

if [ "A${2}" != "A" ]
then
  if [ "${2}" != "-s" ]
  then
    Usage ${2}
    exit 6
  fi
fi

# removes any whitespace/new line/carriage returns
SERVER_STATUS=`curl -s $PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL`
SERVER_STATUS="$(echo -e "${SERVER_STATUS}" | tr -d '[[:space:]]')"

if [ "A${SERVER_STATUS}" == "A" ]
then
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "ERROR! ${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) did not respond at all"
  fi
  exit 2
elif [ "${SERVER_STATUS}" == "0" ]
then
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) webservice is up"
  fi
  exit 0
elif [ "${SERVER_STATUS}" == "1" ]
then
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) CorrectAddress Data is out of date, cannot verify any addresses"
  fi
  exit 1
elif [ "${SERVER_STATUS}" == "2" ]
then
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) webservice is down"
  fi
  exit 2
elif [ "${SERVER_STATUS}" == "3" ]
then
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) webservice is down, unknown exception"
  fi
  exit 3
else
  if [ "A${2}" == "A" ]
  then
    echo "ERROR! ${1} ($PROTO://$HOST:$PORT/$CONTEXT/$URL) returned invalid response"
    echo "  \"${SERVER_STATUS}\""
  fi
  exit 4
fi

exit 0

#check_fs.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl

use Data::Dumper;

$fs = {
	'/oracle' => '6006016021F616001E33151F99E6DA11',
	'/ds' => '6006016021F616006EB157B5CCDEDA11',
	'/fast1' => '6006016021F61600708D418CC9DEDA11',
	'/oracle_logs' => '6006016021F6160071B157B5CCDEDA11',
	'/med2' => '6006016021F61600B6D01A2FC4DEDA11',
	'/med1' => '6006016021F61600F8FB1819C4DEDA11'
};


foreach $sys (qw/ds01 ds02 ds03 ds04 ds05 ds13/)
{

	print "Working on system $sys\n";

	print "     Getting Mount Info\n";

	system("ssh -q $sys mount > /tmp/info_mount_$sys.dat");

	open (DATA, "< /tmp/info_mount_$sys.dat") || die $!;

	while (<DATA>)
	{
		chomp;
		next if (! /emcpower/);
		@data = split("[ ]+", $_);

		$data[0] =~ s/^.*\///;

		$mount->{$sys}->{$data[0]} = $data[2];
	}

	close (DATA);

	print "     Getting Mount Info\n";

	system("ssh -q $sys /sbin/powermt display dev=all > /tmp/info_powermt_$sys.dat");

	open (DATA, "< /tmp/info_powermt_$sys.dat") || die $!;

	$device = "";
	while (<DATA>)
	{
		chomp;
		if (/Pseudo name=([^\s]+)/)
		{
			$device = $1;
			$device_id = "";
			$name = "";
		}

		if (/Logical device ID=([^\s]+)\s+[[](.*)[]]/)
		{
			$device_id = $1;
			$name = $2;


			if (exists($mount->{$sys}->{$device}))
			{
				$fs_name = $mount->{$sys}->{$device};
				if ($device_id eq $fs->{$fs_name})
				{
					print "$sys:$device:$device_id:$name:$mount->{$sys}->{$device}:Good\n";
				}
				else
				{
					print "$sys:$device:$device_id:$name:$mount->{$sys}->{$device}:Cross Mounted!\n";
				}
			}
			else
			{
				print "$sys:$device:$device_id:$name:$mount->{$sys}->{$device}:Not mounted!\n";
			}
	

			$powermt->{$sys}->{$device} = $name;
		}
	}

	close (DATA);

}

#check_users.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl

use Data::Dumper;
use Params::Validate qw(:all);

use strict;
use warnings;

our @all_systems = (qw/ds01 ds02 ds03 ds04 ds05 ds13/);
our $ssh = "ssh -q";

our $required = {
		GROUP => {	bluegrp	=>	{ 	gid		=>	761,
																users =>	[ qw/hp-nonstop ds bluelite cps/ ] },
																bshare	=>	{ 	gid		=>	762,
																users =>	[ qw/ds bluelite/ ] },
								dba			=>	{ 	gid		=>	503,
																users =>	[ qw/bluelite oracle/ ] }
							},
		USER	=> {	oracle		=> {	uid						=> 502,
																default_group	=> 'dba',
																groups				=> [ ],
																comment				=> 'Oracle Administrator' },
								bluelite	=> {	uid						=> 502,
																default_group	=> 'bluegrp',
																groups				=> [ qw/bshare users dba/],
																comment				=> 'Oracle Administrator' }
							}
	};

our $groupmod = "/usr/sbin/groupmod";
our $groupadd = "/usr/sbin/groupadd";
our $useradd = "/usr/sbin/useradd";
our $usermod = "/usr/sbin/usermod";

our $current = {};

sub group_name ($$)
{
	my $group_id = shift;
	my $system = shift;
	my $group_name;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "group_name: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if ($group_id !~ /^\d+$/)
	{
		print STDERR "group_name: Group ID \"$group_id\" is not a group_id\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	foreach $group_name (keys %{$current->{$system}->{GROUP}})
	{
		if ($current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$group_name}->{gid} == $group_id)
		{
			return $group_name;
		}
	}
	return undef;
}

sub group_id ($$)
{
	my $group_name = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "group_id: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! exists($current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$group_name}))
	{
		print STDERR "Unknown group \"$group_name\" on system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	return $current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$group_name}->{gid};
}

sub group_exists ($$)
{
	my $group = shift;
	my $system = shift;
	my $group_name;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "group_exists: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if ($group =~ /^\d+$/)
	{

		foreach $group_name (keys %{$current->{$system}->{GROUP}})
		{
			if ($current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$group_name}->{gid} == $group)
			{
				return 1;
			}
		}

	}
	else
	{

		if (exists($current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$group}))
		{
			return 1;
		}
	}

	return 0;

}

sub user_exists ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;
	my $user_name;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "user_exists: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if ($user =~ /^\d+$/)
	{
		foreach $user_name (keys %{$current->{$system}->{USER}})
		{
			if ($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user_name}->{uid} == $user)
			{
				return 1;
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		if (exists($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user}))
		{
			return 1;
		}
	}

	return 0;

}

sub user_name ($$)
{
	my $user_id = shift;
	my $system = shift;
	my $user_name;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "user_name: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	foreach $user_name (keys %{$current->{$system}->{USER}})
	{
		if ($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user_name}->{uid} == $user_id)
		{
			return $user_name;
		}
	}
	return undef;
}

sub user_id ($$)
{
	my $user_name = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "user_id: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! exists($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user_name}))
	{
		print STDERR "Unknown user \"$user_name\" on system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	return $current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user_name}->{uid};
}


sub user_info ($$$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;
	my $info = shift;
	my $user_name;

	my $the_user_name;

	if (! exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		print STDERR "user_exists: Unknown system \"$system\"\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if ($user =~ /^\d+$/)
	{
		foreach $user_name (keys %{$current->{$system}->{USER}})
		{
			if ($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user_name}->{uid} == $user)
			{
				$the_user_name = $user_name;
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		if (exists($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user}))
		{
			$the_user_name = $user;
		}
	}

	if (! defined($the_user_name))
	{
		#print STDERR "user_$info: Cannot locate the user \"$user\" on system $system\n";
		return "";
	}


	return defined($current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user}->{$info}) ? $current->{$system}->{USER}->{$user}->{$info} : "";

}

sub user_comment ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	return user_info($user, $system, 'comment');
}

sub user_default_group ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	return user_info($user, $system, 'default_gid');

}

sub user_passwd ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	return user_info($user, $system, 'passwd');
}

sub user_homedir ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	return user_info($user, $system, 'homedir');
}

sub user_login_prog ($$)
{
	my $user = shift;
	my $system = shift;

	return user_info($user, $system, 'login_prog');
}

sub info_collected($)
{
my $system = shift;

	if (exists($current->{$system}))
	{
		return 1;
	}
	else
	{
		return 0;
	}
}

sub collect_user_and_group_info($)
{
my $system = shift;
my ($username, $passwd, $uid, $default_gid, $comment, $gid, $homedir, $login_prog);
my ($groupname, $users_field, $users);

	delete($current->{$system});
 
	print "Collecting user and group information from system $system\n";

	open (DATA, "$ssh -q $system cat /etc/passwd |" ) || die $!;

	while (<DATA>)
	{
		chomp;
		next if (! /[:].*[:]/);
		($username, $passwd, $uid, $default_gid, $comment, $homedir, $login_prog) = split("[:]", $_);

		$current->{$system}->{USER}->{$username} = {	uid						=>	$uid,
																									default_gid		=> $default_gid,
																									comment				=> $comment,
																									homedir				=> $homedir,
																									login_prog		=> $login_prog } ;
	}

	close (DATA);

	open (DATA, "$ssh -q $system cat /etc/group |" ) || die $!;

	while (<DATA>)
	{
		chomp;
		next if (! /[:].*[:]/);
		($groupname, $passwd, $gid, $users_field) = split("[:]", $_);
		@{$users} = split(",", $users_field);

		$current->{$system}->{GROUP}->{$groupname} = {	gid						=>	$gid,
																								users					=>	$users};

	}

	close (DATA);

	open (DATA, "$ssh -q $system cat /etc/shadow |" ) || die $!;

	while (<DATA>)
	{
		chomp;
		next if (! /[:].*[:]/);
		($username, $passwd) = split("[:]", $_, 3);

		$current->{$system}->{USER}->{$username}->{passwd} = $passwd;

	}

	close (DATA);


#	print "DUMP of $system\n";
#	print Dumper ($current->{$system});
}

sub update_group($;@)
{
	my %option;
	my $group_id;
	my $group_name;
	my @systems;
	my $system;

	%option = validate_with
							( params  => \@_,
								spec    => {  group_id			=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															sys						=>  { type => SCALAR|ARRAYREF, optional => 1 },
															group_name		=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 }
							},
								called  => 'update group',
								normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^-//; return uc $k }
							);

	if (! exists($option{GROUP_ID}))
	{
		print STDERR "update_group: No group id given\n";
		exit(1);
	}
	$group_id = $option{GROUP_ID};

	if (! exists($option{GROUP_NAME}))
	{
		print STDERR "update_group: No group name given\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$group_name = $option{GROUP_NAME};

	if (exists($option{SYS}))
	{
		if (ref($option{SYS}) eq "ARRAY")
		{
			@systems = @{$option{SYS}};
		}
		else
		{
			@systems = split (",", $option{SYS});
			foreach (@systems) { s/^\s+//; s/\s*$//; } ;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		@systems = @all_systems;
	}

print "SYSTEMS: " . join(", ", @systems) . "\n";

	foreach $system (@systems)
	{

		if (! info_collected($system))
		{
			collect_user_and_group_info($system);
		}
			
		if (group_exists($group_name, $system))
		{

			# Check if the group is correct

			if (group_id($group_name, $system) != $group_id) 
			{
			
				# Mod the group
				print "Mod group $group_id ($group_name) to system $system\n";

				if (group_exists($group_id, $system))
				{
					printf STDERR "update_group: Unable to change group \"%s\" id from %s to %s on system $system because that group_id already exists as \"%s\"\n", 
										$group_name,
										group_id($group_name, $system),
										$group_id,
										group_name($group_id, $system);
				}
				else
				{
					print "CMD: $ssh $system $groupmod -g $group_id $group_name\n";
				}
			}
			else
			{
				printf "group_mod: Group \"%s\" is correct on system \"%s\" with id of %s\n",
							$group_name,
							$system,
							$group_id;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			# Add the group
			print "Add group $group_id ($group_name) to system $system\n";
			print "CMD: $ssh $system $groupadd -f -g $group_id $group_name\n";
		}
	}
}

sub update_user($;@)
{
	my %option;
	my $user_id;
	my $user_name;
	my @systems;
	my $system;
	my @groups;
	my $mod;
	my $add_user;
	my $required_option;

	%option = validate_with
							( params  => \@_,
								spec    => {  user_id					=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															sys							=>  { type => SCALAR|ARRAYREF, optional => 1 },
															homedir					=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															user_name				=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															login_prog						=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															comment					=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															passwd					=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															default_group		=>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
															groups					=>  { type => SCALAR|ARRAYREF, optional => 1 }
							},
								called  => 'update user',
								normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^-//; return uc $k }
							);


	if (! exists($option{USER_NAME}))
	{
		print STDERR "update_user: No user name given\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$user_name = $option{USER_NAME};

	if ($user_name eq "root")
	{
		print STDERR "Very unwilling to modify the root user - what are you doing?\n";
		exit(1);	
	}



	print "CMD:\n";
	print "CMD:# Configuring user $user_name\n";
	print "CMD:\n";


	if (exists($option{SYS}))
	{
		if (ref($option{SYS}) eq "ARRAY")
		{
			@systems = @{$option{SYS}};
		}
		else
		{
			@systems = split (",", $option{SYS});
			foreach (@systems) { s/^\s+//; s/\s*$//; } ;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		@systems = @all_systems;
	}

	if (exists($option{GROUPS}))
	{
		if (ref($option{GROUPS}) eq "ARRAY")
		{
			@groups = @{$option{GROUPS}};
		}
		else
		{
			@groups = split (",", $option{GROUPS});
			foreach (@groups) { s/^\s+//; s/\s*$//; } ;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		@groups = ();
	}

	if (defined($option{LOGIN_PROG}))
	{
		if ($option{LOGIN_PROG} =~ /^\s*no\s?login\s*$/i)
		{
			$option{LOGIN_PROG} = "/sbin/nologin";
		}
		elsif ($option{LOGIN_PROG} =~ /^\s*bash\s*$/i)
		{
			$option{LOGIN_PROG} = "/bin/bash";
		}
	}

	foreach $system (@systems)
	{

		if (! info_collected($system))
		{
			collect_user_and_group_info($system);
		}

		if (user_exists($user_name, $system))
		{
			$add_user = 0;
		}
		else
		{
			$add_user = 1;
		}

		# Check if the user is correct

		$mod = "";

		if (defined($option{COMMENT}) && (	$add_user ||
																				user_comment($user_name, $system) ne $option{COMMENT}))
		{
			$mod .= " -c \\'$option{COMMENT}\\'";
		}

		if (defined($option{USER_ID}) && (	$add_user ||
																				user_id($user_name, $system) != $option{USER_ID}) )
		{
		
			if (!$add_user && user_exists($option{USER_ID}, $system))
			{
				printf STDERR "update_user: Unable to change user \"%s\" id from %s to %s on system $system because that user_id already exists as \"%s\"\n", 
									$user_name,
									user_id($user_name, $system),
									$option{USER_ID},
									user_name($option{USER_ID}, $system);
			}
			else
			{
				$mod .= " -u $option{USER_ID}";
			}
		}

print "DEBUG: " . join(", ", user_default_group($user_name, $system), $option{DEFAULT_GROUP}) . "\n";
		if (defined($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}))
		{
			if ($option{DEFAULT_GROUP} =~ /^\d+$/)
			{
print "DEBUG: " . join(", ", user_default_group($user_name, $system), $option{DEFAULT_GROUP}) . "\n";
				if  (	$add_user || user_default_group($user_name, $system) ne $option{DEFAULT_GROUP})
				{
					if (group_exists($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system))
					{
						$mod .= " -g $option{DEFAULT_GROUP}";
					}
					else
					{
						print STDERR "update_user: Cannot modify user's default group to '$option{DEFAULT_GROUP}' because it does not exists on $system\n";
					}
				}
			}
			else
			{
print "DEBUG: " . join(", ", user_default_group($user_name, $system), group_id($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system)) . "\n";
				if  (	$add_user || !group_exists($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system) || user_default_group($user_name, $system) ne group_id($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system))
				{
					if (group_exists($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system))
					{
						$mod .= " -g $option{DEFAULT_GROUP}";
					}
					else
					{
						print STDERR "update_user: Cannot modify user's default group to '$option{DEFAULT_GROUP}' because it does not exists on $system\n";
					}
				}
				elsif (!group_exists($option{DEFAULT_GROUP}, $system))
				{
					print STDERR "update_user: Cannot modify user's default group to '$option{DEFAULT_GROUP}' because it does not exists on $system\n";
				}
			}

		}

		if (defined($option{PASSWD}) && 	(	$add_user ||
																				user_passwd($user_name, $system) ne $option{PASSWD}))
		{
			$mod .= " -p \\'$option{PASSWD}\\'";
		}

		if (defined($option{LOGIN_PROG}) && 	(	$add_user ||
																			user_login_prog($user_name, $system) ne $option{LOGIN_PROG}))
		{
			$mod .= " -s \\'$option{LOGIN_PROG}\\'";
		}

			
		if (! $add_user)
		{

			if ($mod !~ /^\s*$/)
			{
					print "CMD: $ssh $system $usermod $mod $user_name\n";
			}
			else
			{
				printf "user_mod: User \"%s\" is correct on system \"%s\"\n",
							$user_name,
							$system;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			# Add user
			foreach $required_option (qw/USER_ID HOMEDIR LOGIN_PROG PASSWD DEFAULT_GROUP/)
			{
				if (! exists($option{USER_ID}))
				{
					print STDERR "update_user: Option \"$required_option\" required during an add of a user \"$user_name\" on system \"$system\"\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}

			if ($mod !~ /^\s*$/)
			{
				print "CMD: $ssh $system $useradd -n $mod $user_name\n";
			}
			else
			{
				printf "user_mod: User \"%s\" is correct on system \"%s\"\n",
							$user_name,
							$system;
			}
		}
	}
}

#chkmounts
#!/usr/bin/perl

use Data::Dumper;
use Sys::Hostname;

use strict;
use warnings;

our $issue = {};
our $mountinfofilename = "/ds/common/etc/server_mount.info";
our $error_status = 0;


sub read_mount_info($)
{
my $mountinfo = shift;
my 	($server, $mount, $type, $options) ;
my $all;
my $global = {};


if (! -f $mountinfo)
{
	print STDERR "checkmounts: Unable to locate mount info file \"$mountinfo\"\n";
	$error_status = 4;
	goto COMPLETE;
}



if (! open (INFO, "< $mountinfo" ))
{
	print STDERR "checkmounts: Unable to open mount info file \"$mountinfo\"\n";
	print STDERR "error: $!\n";
	$error_status = 4;
	goto COMPLETE;
}

while (<INFO>)
{
	chomp;
	# Remove comments
	s/[#].*$//;
	# Remove whitspace
	s/^\s*//;
	s/\s*$//;
	# Remove blank lines
	next if (/^\s*$/);

	($server, $mount, $type, $options) = split('\s*:\s*', $_);

	next if ($server ne "all");

	$all->{$mount}->{TYPE} = $type;

	if ($options ne "")
	{
		@{$all->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = split(",", $options);
	}
	else
	{
		@{$all->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = ();
	}

}
close (INFO);

if (! open (INFO, "< $mountinfo" ))
{
	print STDERR "checkmounts: Unable to open mount info file \"$mountinfo\"\n";
	print STDERR "error: $!\n";
	$error_status = 4;
	goto COMPLETE;
}

while (<INFO>)
{
	chomp;
	# Remove comments
	s/[#].*$//;
	# Remove whitspace
	s/^\s*//;
	s/\s*$//;
	# Remove blank lines
	next if (/^\s*$/);

	($server, $mount, $type, $options) = split('\s*:\s*', $_);

	next if ($server eq "all");

	$global->{$server}->{$mount}->{TYPE} = $type;

	if ($options ne "")
	{
		@{$global->{$server}->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = split(",", $options);
	}
	else
	{
		@{$global->{$server}->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = ();
	}

}


$global->{STD} = {};

foreach $mount (keys %{$all})
{
	foreach $server (keys %{$global})
	{
		if (! exists($global->{$server}->{$mount}))
		{
			$global->{$server}->{$mount}->{TYPE} = $all->{$mount}->{TYPE};
			@{$global->{$server}->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = @{$all->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}};
		}
	}

}


return $global;

}

sub record ($$;@)
{
	my $hostname = shift;
	my $mount = shift;
	my $level = shift;
	my $message = shift;

	push (@{$issue->{$hostname}->{$mount}},
				{ LEVEL => $level,
					MSG => $message });
}




my $global;
my $hostname;
my $use_hostname;
my @servers;
my $mount;
my $option;
my @option;
my $type;
my @hostnames;
my $open;
my ($device, $options, $dump, $fsck);
my $fstab;
my $error = {};
my $mounted = {};
my @mountinfofiles;
my $ds_msg;
my @test;
my $mount_string;


if (! ($global = read_mount_info($mountinfofilename)))
{
	print STDERR "Unable to read mount info file - Aborting\n";
	$error_status = 4;
	goto COMPLETE;
}

#print Dumper ($global);

if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
{
	@servers = @ARGV;
}
else
{
	@servers = (hostname);
}

# ($host, $aliases, $addrtype, $length, @addrs) = gethostbyname( $host );


foreach $hostname (@servers)
{
	# Get /etc/fstab

	if (hostname eq $hostname || hostname =~ /^$hostname[.]/)
	{

		if (! -r "/etc/fstab")
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot access local /etc/fstab\n";
			next;
		}

		if (! open (FSTAB, "< /etc/fstab"))
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot open local /etc/fstab\n";
			print STDERR "error: $!\n";
			next;
		}
		
	}
	else
	{

		# Test that ssh to the host will work at all

		if (! open (TEST, "ssh -n $hostname echo confirmed  2>&1  |"))
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot open remote ssh on $hostname\n";
			print STDERR "error: $!\n";
			next;
		}

		@test = <TEST>;

		if (! grep { $_ =~ /confirmed/ } @test)
		{
			close (TEST);
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Unable to ssh to host $hostname\n";
			print STDERR "error(s): @test\n";
			$error_status = 4;
			goto COMPLETE;
		}

		close (TEST);
		
		if (! open (FSTAB, "ssh -q $hostname cat /etc/fstab |"))
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot open remote /etc/fstab on $hostname\n";
			print STDERR "error: $!\n";
			next;
		}
	}

	$fstab = {};

	while (<FSTAB>)
	{
		chomp;
		# Remove comments
		s/[#].*$//;
		# Remove whitspace
		s/^\s*//;
		s/\s*$//;
		# Remove blank lines
		next if (/^\s*$/);

		($device, $mount, $type, $options, $dump, $fsck) = split('\s+', $_);

		$fstab->{$mount}->{DEVICE} = $device;
		$fstab->{$mount}->{TYPE} = $type;
		$fstab->{$mount}->{DUMP} = $dump;
		$fstab->{$mount}->{FSCK} = $fsck;
		@{$fstab->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = split(",", $options);

	}

	close (FSTAB);



	if (hostname eq $hostname || hostname =~ /^$hostname[.]/)
	{
		if (! open (MOUNT, "mount |"))
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot exec mount\n";
			print STDERR "error: $!\n";
			next;
		}
		
	}
	else
	{
		if (! open (MOUNT, "ssh -q $hostname mount |"))
		{
			print STDERR "chkmounts: Cannot run remote mount on $hostname\n";
			print STDERR "error: $!\n";
			next;
		}
	}

	$mount = {};

	while (<MOUNT>)
	{
		chomp;
		# Remove comments
		s/[#].*$//;
		# Remove whitspace
		s/^\s*//;
		s/\s*$//;
		# Remove blank lines
		next if (/^\s*$/);

		if (/^(\S+)\s+on\s+(\S+)\s+type\s+(\S+)\s+[(](\S+)[)]/)
		{
			($device, $mount, $type, $options) = ($1, $2, $3, $4);
		}
		elsif (/^(\S+)\s+on\s+(\S+)\s+type\s+(\S+)/)
		{
			($device, $mount, $type) = ($1, $2, $3);
		}
		else
		{
			record("GLOBAL", "GLOBAL", 1,
							"chkmounts ($hostname) - Can't parse mount output line: $_");
		}

		$mounted->{$mount}->{DEVICE} = $device;
		$mounted->{$mount}->{TYPE} = $type;
		@{$mounted->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}} = split(",", $options);

	}

	close (MOUNT);




	$use_hostname = $hostname;

	if (! exists($global->{$use_hostname}))
	{
		$use_hostname =~ s/[.].*$//;

		if (! exists($global->{$use_hostname}))
		{
			# Can find a reference to current hostname so I'll use the standard one

			$use_hostname = "STD";

			if (! exists($global->{$use_hostname}))
			{
				print STDERR "chkmounts: Don't have mounts for servers not referenced in mount info file - assuming no mounts\n";
				$global->{$hostname} = {}; # No mounts
				$use_hostname = $hostname;			
			}
		}
		
	}


	# Check Mounts

	foreach $mount (keys %{$global->{$use_hostname}})
	{
		if (exists($fstab->{$mount}))
		{
			if ($fstab->{$mount}->{TYPE} ne $global->{$use_hostname}->{$mount}->{TYPE})
			{
	
				record($hostname, $mount, 3,
							"Mount \"$mount\" - required type of \"$global->{$use_hostname}->{$mount}->{TYPE}\" different than current \"$fstab->{$mount}->{TYPE}\" in /etc/fstab");
			}

			foreach $option (@{$global->{$use_hostname}->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}})
			{
				if (! grep { $_ eq $option } @{$fstab->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}})
				{
					if ($option eq "ro")
					{
						record($hostname, $mount, 3,
							"Mount \"$mount\" - required readonly option not active - options = \"" . join(",", @{$fstab->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}}) . "\"");
					}
					else
					{
						record($hostname, $mount, 2,
							"Mount \"$mount\" - required option of \"$option\" not active - options = \"" . join(",", @{$fstab->{$mount}->{OPTIONS}}) . "\"");
					}
				}
				
			}

			if (exists($mounted->{$mount}))
			{
				$mount_string = $mount;
				$mount_string =~ s!^.*[/]!!;

				opendir(DIR, $mount) || die "can't opendir $mount: $!";
    		@mountinfofiles = grep { -f "$mount/$_" && $_ =~ /^fs_.*[.]info$/} readdir(DIR);
    		closedir DIR;
#print "MOUNT: $mount\n";
#print Dumper (\@mountinfofiles);

				if (scalar(@mountinfofiles) == 0)
				{
					# No fs.*.info file on this filesystem - assume that is ok
					record($hostname, $mount, 1,
						"Mount \"$mount\" does not appear to have a fs_XXXX.info file on the mount root");
				}
				elsif (grep { s/^fs_//; s/[.]info$//; $_ eq $mount_string } @mountinfofiles)
				{
					1; # OK
				}
				else
				{
					record($hostname, $mount, 3,
						"Mount \"$mount\" is cross mounted to " . join(" or ", @mountinfofiles) . "!!! Unmount now!!!");
				}
				
			
			}
			else
			{
				record($hostname, $mount, 3,
					"Mount \"$mount\" is not mounted!");
			}
			
				
		}
		else
		{
			record($hostname, $mount, 3,
				"Mount \"$mount\" not in /etc/fstab as required on server \"$hostname\"");
		}


	}

	



}


COMPLETE:


foreach $hostname (sort keys %{$issue})
{
	print "Server $hostname Issues\n";
	print "=======================================\n";
	foreach $mount (sort keys %{$issue->{$hostname}})
	{
		foreach $ds_msg (sort { $a->{LEVEL} <=> $b->{LEVEL} } @{$issue->{$hostname}->{$mount}})
		{
			print "    ($ds_msg->{LEVEL}) $ds_msg->{MSG}\n";
			if ($ds_msg->{LEVEL} > $error_status)
			{
				$error_status = $ds_msg->{LEVEL};
			}
		}
		print "\n";
	}
}


print STDERR "\n";

if ($error_status == 0)
{
	print STDERR "chk_mounts($error_status): Successful check of filesystems with no issues\n";
}
elsif ($error_status == 1)
{
	print STDERR "chk_mounts($error_status): Minor issues detected - please notify Data Services via Email\n";
}
elsif ($error_status == 2)
{
	print STDERR "chk_mounts($error_status): Medium level issues detected - please notify Data Services via Email\n";
}
elsif ($error_status == 3)
{
	print STDERR "chk_mounts($error_status): Major issues detected - please notify Data Services immediately\n";
}
else
{
	print STDERR "chk_mounts($error_status): Check Mount program was unable to execute successfully - please notify Data Services immediately\n";
}



exit($error_status);




#code_changes
#!/usr/bin/bash

########################################################################
#  ____ ___  ____  _____    ____ _   _    _    _   _  ____ _____ ____  
# / ___/ _ \|  _ \| ____|  / ___| | | |  / \  | \ | |/ ___| ____/ ___| 
#| |  | | | | | | |  _|   | |   | |_| | / _ \ |  \| | |  _|  _| \___ \ 
#| |__| |_| | |_| | |___  | |___|  _  |/ ___ \| |\  | |_| | |___ ___) |
# \____\___/|____/|_____|  \____|_| |_/_/   \_\_| \_|\____|_____|____/ 
#########################################################################

# Program: code_changes - Report Data Services code changes
# Author: William Hampton, CoverMyMeds

# Version 1.0 - 05/17/2024


display_usage() {
echo "Usage: The focus of this script is to search for code/config changes."
}

# Check whether user had supplied -h or --help . If yes display usage
if [[ ( $@ == "--help") ||  $@ == "-h" ]]
 then
     display_usage
     exit 0
fi


days=$1

# Find Changes
ds_prod=$(find /ds/production/ -maxdepth 4 -path '*/bin/*' -mtime $days -type f  2>&1 | grep -v "Permission denied" | grep -v "no such file") 

env_prod1=$(find /ds/env/prod/ -maxdepth 4 -path '*/common/bin/*' -mtime $days -type f  2>&1 -o -path '*/common/etc*' -name "*xml" -mtime $days 2>&1 | grep -v "Permission denied" | grep -v "no such file") 

env_prod2=$(find /ds/env/prod/ -path '*/common/lib/*' -mtime $days -type f  2>&1 -o -path '*/util/bin*' -mtime $days -type f 2>&1 | grep -v "Permission denied" | grep -v "no such file")

c="${ds_prod} ${env_prod1} ${env_prod2}"



if [ -n "$c" ]; then
	 mail -s "Data Services Changes" william.hampton@mckesson.com, christine.howard@relayhealth.com  <<< "$c"
fi

#compress_old_logs


days=60
echo $LOG_DIR
if [ ! -d "$LOG_DIR" ]
  then
		echo LOG_DIR not set to a existing directory!
		exit 1
fi

echo Storage on $LOG_DIR :
df -h $LOG_DIR

echo Compressing .log files not modified within the last $days days

time find $LOG_DIR -mtime +$days -name '*.log' -exec bzip2 --best {} \;

echo Completed

echo Storage on $LOG_DIR :
df -h $LOG_DIR
