#create_al_index
#!/usr/bin/perl

# al_index_manager: Audit Log Index Manager
# This is a command-line interface to the BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr modules
#
# Author: jmh
#
# Version history:
# 1/10/2006 - Initial release
# 6/4/2007  - Added completion email capability
# 2/2/2016  - Added 'prune_al_index' capability to clean down indexes by retention period 

use warnings;
use strict;

use Data::Dumper;
use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use Mail::SendEasy;

our $VERSION = '1.1';
our $TEMP_DIR = $ENV{TMPDIR};	# temp files for building indexes will go here

our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
our $SMTP_SERVER = $ENV{DEFAULT_SMTP_SERVER};

die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

initialize_logging(logfile => "$DS_BASE_DIR/common/log/al_index_mgr.$$.log", screen_only => 0, screen_threshold => 'ERROR', file_threshold => 'ERROR');

my %params_date_spec_required = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Mandatory range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 0
	}
);

my %params_date_spec_optional = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Optional range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 1
	}
);

my %params_index_spec_required = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 0 } );
my %params_index_spec_optional = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );
my %params_connection_var = ( connection_var => { description => 'Name of environment variable for database connection', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_agg_buckets_optional = ( agg_buckets => { description => 'Number of work units to spread aggregation phase over (e.g. 10, 20, 35, etc)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '35' } );

#my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

#my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_build_priority_spec = ( build_priority => { description => "CPU scheduling priority (nice value from 0 to 19)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '19' } );

#my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx:2' } );
my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_index_profile_attributes = (
                description         =>  { description => 'Description of index (duh)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                field_id            =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP field id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                segment_id          =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP segment id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_function  =>  { description => 'Name of BLUELITE::Normalize function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_params    =>  { description => 'Parameters for normalize_function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                valid_only_ind      =>  { description => "Set to 1 to limit indexing to 'valid' values when using normalize_function", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                hash_method         =>  { description => "Name of BLUELITE::Normalize hash_method to apply (e.g. 'crc16')", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_begin  =>  { description => 'First process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_end    =>  { description => 'Last process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1}
);

our $script_name = $0;
$script_name =~ s|.*/||g;	# get basename

our $command_meta = {

	build_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index (unconditional)',

		param_validation => {
			%params_date_spec_required,
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&build_al_index
	},

	create_al_index => {
		description => 'Define profile for new index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&create_al_index
	},

	drop_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove all index data and profile',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&drop_al_index
	},

	enable_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index only on process dates not yet enabled',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&enable_al_index
	},

	remove_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove index data',	

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&remove_al_index
	},
	
	update_al_index => {
		description => 'Update profile for existing index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&update_al_index
	},
	
	prune_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove expired process dates for existing indexes',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
		},

		method => \&prune_al_index
	},
};


sub general_usage() {

	print "$script_name version $VERSION\n";
	print "Usage:                         $script_name -email addresses -command -command_parameters\n";
	print "Alternate (equivalent) usage:  command -command_parameters\n\n";
	print "Supported commands are:\n\n";

	foreach my $command (keys %{$command_meta}) {
		print "$command	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{description} . "\n";
	}

	print "\nTo get command-specific help use '$script_name -command -help'  or  'command -help'\n";
}

sub command_usage($) {
  my $command = shift;

	print "Usage: $command -parameters\n";
	print "\nRequired parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && (! $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "\nOptional parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if ((! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) ||
			(exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})
		) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "	-email	Comma-seperated list of email addresses to send to upon completion\n";
}


my $command;

if (! exists($command_meta->{$script_name})) {
	$command = lc(shift @ARGV);
	$command =~ s/^--?//;

	if (($command =~ /^-?-?help/i) or ($command eq '')) {
		general_usage;
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! exists($command_meta->{$command})) {
		die "ERROR: Command '$command' is not supported by the index manager\n";
	}
} else {
	$command = $script_name;
}

if (! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation})) {
	die "ERROR: Command '$command' has no 'param_validation' info in source code!\n";
}

if ((! defined($ARGV[0])) or ($ARGV[0] =~ /^-?-?help/i)) {
	command_usage($command);
	exit(1);
}

my %option = validate_with (
	params  => \@ARGV,
	spec    => {
							%{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}},
							email => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 }
							},
	called  => $command,
	normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^--?//; return uc $k }
);


our @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS = ();
if (exists($option{CONNECTION_VAR})) {
	push(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS, connection_var => $option{CONNECTION_VAR});
	delete $option{CONNECTION_VAR};
}

#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;

our $index_mgr = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr->new(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

if (! defined($index_mgr)) {
	die "ERROR: Unable to get new object from BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr\n";
}

##############################################

sub create_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->new_index_profile(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create new index profile object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($index_profile->save_index_profile));

	return 1;
}


sub prune_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  
	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, uc($option->{INDEX_ID}))) {
				
    my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);
    
	  if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
	  	die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object for index : '$index_id'\n";
	  }
		
	  return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));
	  print "\n";
	}
	
	return 1;
}


sub update_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  my $parallel_hosts;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not load existing index profile object\n";
	}

	if (defined($option{PARALLEL_HOSTS})) {
		$parallel_hosts = $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
		delete $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
	}

	$index_profile->save_index_profile(%{$option});

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (defined($parallel_hosts)) {
		$maint_grp->parallel_hosts($parallel_hosts);
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));

	return 1;
}


sub index_ids_to_objects($) {
  my $index_ids = shift;
  my %index_list;

	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, $index_ids)) {

		$index_list{$index_id} = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

		if (! defined($index_list{$index_id})) {
			die "ERROR: Could not obtain index object for index_id '$index_id'\n";
		}

	}

	return %index_list;
}


sub convert_process_dates($) {
  my $options = shift;
  my (%process_dates);

	if (defined($options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
		foreach my $element (split(/[,\s]+/, $options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
			if ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				$process_dates{$1} = 1;

			} elsif ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*-\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				if (! exists($options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN})) {
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN} = $1;
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_END} = $2;
				} else {
					die "ERROR: Currently, only 1 process date range may be specified\n";
				}

			} else {
				die "ERROR: process date spec of '$element' is not valid\n";
			}
		}

		if (scalar(keys %process_dates) >= 1) {
			@{$options->{PROCESS_DATES}} = (sort keys %process_dates);
		}

		delete $options->{PROCESS_DATE};
	}

	return $options;
}


sub build_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->rebuild));

	return 1;
}


sub enable_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, temp_dir => $TEMP_DIR, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	# get a list of all defined indexes if none specified on command line

	if (! exists($option->{INDEX_ID})) {
		foreach my $index_id ($index_mgr->all_indexes) {
			$maint_grp->add_index($index_id);
		}
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->enable));

	return 1;
}


sub remove_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return $maint_grp->delete;
}


sub drop_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
	my %indexes = index_ids_to_objects($option->{INDEX_ID});
  my $undeleted_profiles = 0;
#print "HEY\n";
#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;
  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (! $maint_grp->delete) {
		return undef;
	}

	foreach my $index_id (keys %indexes) {

		if (! $indexes{$index_id}->delete_index_profile) {

			print STDERR "ERROR: All index data deleted for index '$index_id', but unable to remove it's index profile definition from database\n";
			$undeleted_profiles++;
		}
	}

	if ($undeleted_profiles) {
		return undef;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}


sub email(@) {

  my $mail = new Mail::SendEasy( smtp => $SMTP_SERVER);

  if (! defined($mail) ) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to establish a SMTP connection to $SMTP_SERVER\n";
    return undef;
  }

  my $status = $mail->send(
    from => 'data.services@relayhealth.com',
    from_title => 'RelayHealth Data Services',
    @_
  );

  if (! $status) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Failed to be send email\n";
    return undef;
  }

  return 1;
}


##############################################

my ($exit_status, $email);

if (defined($option{EMAIL})) {
	$email = $option{EMAIL};
	delete $option{EMAIL};
}

if ((exists($command_meta->{$command}->{method})) && (exists(&{$command_meta->{$command}->{method}}))) {
	my $ret;

	eval { $ret = $command_meta->{$command}->{method}(\%option) };

	warn $@ if $@;

  my $completion_status;

	if (! defined($ret)) {
		$exit_status = 1;
		$completion_status = 'failed';
	} else {
		$exit_status = 0;
		$completion_status = 'succeeded';
	}

	if (defined($email)) {

		my $option_list = Dumper(\%option);
		$option_list =~ s/\$VAR1/options/;

		email(
			to => $email,
			subject => "$command process $completion_status",
			msg => "The following $command process ${completion_status}:\n\n$option_list\n" . join("\n", $@) . "\n"
		);
	}

	exit($exit_status);
} else {
	die "ERROR: Interface for '$command' not yet supported\n";
}



#create_audit_logs.sh
#!/bin/sh

#####################################
# B.Oliver
# 11-30-22
# create_audit_logs.sh
# Will create audit logs for next year
######################################


t_NEXT_YEAR=$(date -d "$THIS_YEAR +1 year" +%Y)

 cd /dsmounts/ds/data_sources/audit_logs/ || exit

 if [ -L "/dsmounts/xfs20/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""01" ];then

         echo -e "Audit directory already exists, please check" |  mail -s "Audit directory already exists "/dsmounts/xfs20/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""01"" DataServicesNotification@mckesson.com 

 else
    ln -s /dsmounts/xfs20/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"01
    mkdir /dsmounts/xfs20/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"01

fi
 
if [ -L "/dsmounts/xfs21/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""02" ];then

         echo -e "Audit directory already exists, please check" |  mail -s "Audit directory already exists "/dsmounts/xfs21/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""02"" DataServicesNotification@mckesson.com

 else
    ln -s /dsmounts/xfs21/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"02
    mkdir /dsmounts/xfs21/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"02

fi

if [ -L "/dsmounts/comp01/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""03" ];then

         echo -e "Audit directory already exists, please check" |  mail -s "Audit directory already exists "/dsmounts/comp01/data_sources/audit_logs/""$t_NEXT_YEAR""03"" DataServicesNotification@mckesson.com

 else
    ln -s /dsmounts/comp01/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"03
    mkdir /dsmounts/comp01/data_sources/audit_logs/"$t_NEXT_YEAR"03

fi

#csv2excel
#!/usr/bin/perl



use Spreadsheet::WriteExcel::Big;
use Getopt::Long;
use IO;
use File::Spec;
use Text::ParseWords;


sub write_custom() {
  my($worksheet) = shift;

	return $worksheet->write_string(@_);
}

sub new_worksheet($$;$)
{
my ($workbook) = shift;
my ($worksheet_name) = shift;
my ($style) = shift;


				$worksheet_name =~ s/[.](dat|csv|txt)([.]gz)?$//;

				if (length($worksheet_name) > 31)
				{
					$worksheet_name =~ s/[_0-9]+$//;
					$worksheet_name = substr($worksheet_name, 0, 31);
				}

				$worksheet = $workbook->add_worksheet($worksheet_name);

				$worksheet->keep_leading_zeros();
				$worksheet->freeze_panes(1, 0);
				$worksheet->set_landscape();
#				$worksheet->set_margins(0.1) ;
				$worksheet->repeat_rows(0);
				$worksheet->fit_to_pages(1, 0); # 1 page wide and as long as necessary

				if (! $LOOKS_LIKE) {
					$worksheet->add_write_handler(qr/^.*$/, \&write_custom);
				}

				return $worksheet;

}

$heading = 0;
$delimiter = ",";
$data_quoted = 0;

$style = "PRESENTATION";
$LOOKS_LIKE = 0;

$ret = GetOptions(  "heading|h!" => \$heading,
										"delimiter|d=s" => \$delimiter,
										"data_quoted" => \$data_quoted,
										"data", sub { $style = "DATA"},
										"looks_like", sub { $LOOKS_LIKE = 1 }
 );

  if (! $ret)
  {
    exit(1);
  }

if ($delimiter =~ /tab/i)
{
	$delimiter = chr(9);
}

$delimiter = '\\' . $delimiter;

sub usage()
{
	print STDERR "\n";
	print STDERR "  csv2excel [--looks_like] [ --[no]heading ] [-- data_quoted] [--delimiter=c] excelfile.xls delimited_file [ ... delimited_file ]\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	print STDERR "\n";


}
if (scalar(@ARGV) > 0)
{

	$excel_file = shift (@ARGV);

	if ($excel_file !~ /[.]xls$/)
	{
		print STDERR "The excel file does not have .xls extension\n";
		exit(1);
	}
}
else
{
	usage();
	exit(1);
}

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0)
{
	print STDERR "No delimited files specified\n";
	exit(1);

}


my $workbook = Spreadsheet::WriteExcel::Big->new($excel_file);

if (! $workbook)
{
	print STDERR "Failed to open Excel file\n";
	exit(1);
}

%heading_format_hash = ( bold => 1, color => 'navy', bg_color => 'yellow', align => 'general', valign => 'bottom', text_wrap => 1 );

if ($style eq "DATA")
{
	%data_format_hash = ( bold => 0, color => 'black', align => 'text', valign => 'top', text_wrap => 1, shrink => 1, font  => 'Courier New');
}
else
{
	%data_format_hash = ( bold => 0, color => 'black', align => 'text', valign => 'top', text_wrap => 1, shrink => 1);
}

if (! $LOOKS_LIKE) {
	$data_format_hash{num_format} = '@';
}

$heading_format = $workbook->add_format(%heading_format_hash);

$heading_format->set_top(1);
$heading_format->set_bottom(1);
$heading_format->set_left(1);
$heading_format->set_right(1);

$data_format    = $workbook->add_format(%data_format_hash);
$data_format->set_top(1);
$data_format->set_bottom(1);
$data_format->set_left(1);
$data_format->set_right(1);


foreach $delimited_file (@ARGV)
{

$worksheet_name = (File::Spec->splitpath($delimited_file))[2];
$worksheet_name =~ s/[.](dat|csv|txt)([.]gz)?$//;



# Add a worksheet
$worksheet = new_worksheet($workbook, $worksheet_name, $style);

print STDERR "Reading file " . (File::Spec->splitpath($delimited_file))[2] . " into the worksheet " . $worksheet->get_name() . "\n";

$worksheet_part = 1;

if ($delimited_file =~ /[.](gz|zip)$/)
{
	$open_cmd = "gunzip -c $delimited_file |";
}
else
{
	$open_cmd = "< $delimited_file";
}

if (! open(DATA, "$open_cmd"))
{
	print STDERR "Unable to open the file \"$delimited_file\"\n";
	exit(1);
}

	$row = 0;
	while (<DATA>)
	{
		s/\015?\012$//;

		if ($row > 65500)
		{
			$worksheet_part++;
			$worksheet = new_worksheet($workbook, $worksheet_name . $worksheet_part, $style);

			print STDERR "  Continued to the next tab with the same file due to size (tab is " . $worksheet_name . $worksheet_part . ")\n";
			$row = 0;
		}

		$excel_row = [];

		s/'/\\'/g;

		if ($data_quoted)
		{
			@{$excel_row} = &parse_line($delimiter, 0, $_);
		}
		else
		{
			@{$excel_row} = split('[' . $delimiter . ']', $_);
		}

		if ($row == 0)
		{
			$worksheet->write_row($row, 0, $excel_row, $heading_format);
		}
		else
		{
			$worksheet->write_row($row, 0, $excel_row, $data_format);
		}

	$row++;
	}

	$worksheet->set_column(0, scalar(@{$excel_row}) - 1,  25);


close (DATA);


}

$workbook->close();

#c_rehash
#!/usr/bin/perl


# Perl c_rehash script, scan all files in a directory
# and add symbolic links to their hash values.

my $openssl;

my $dir = "/ds/common/openssl";

if(defined $ENV{OPENSSL}) {
	$openssl = $ENV{OPENSSL};
} else {
	$openssl = "openssl";
	$ENV{OPENSSL} = $openssl;
}

$ENV{PATH} .= ":$dir/bin";

if(! -x $openssl) {
	my $found = 0;
	foreach (split /:/, $ENV{PATH}) {
		if(-x "$_/$openssl") {
			$found = 1;
			last;
		}	
	}
	if($found == 0) {
		print STDERR "c_rehash: rehashing skipped ('openssl' program not available)\n";
		exit 0;
	}
}

if(@ARGV) {
	@dirlist = @ARGV;
} elsif($ENV{SSL_CERT_DIR}) {
	@dirlist = split /:/, $ENV{SSL_CERT_DIR};
} else {
	$dirlist[0] = "$dir/certs";
}


foreach (@dirlist) {
	if(-d $_ and -w $_) {
		hash_dir($_);
	}
}

sub hash_dir {
	my %hashlist;
	print "Doing $_[0]\n";
	chdir $_[0];
	opendir(DIR, ".");
	my @flist = readdir(DIR);
	# Delete any existing symbolic links
	foreach (grep {/^[\da-f]+\.r{0,1}\d+$/} @flist) {
		if(-l $_) {
			unlink $_;
		}
	}
	closedir DIR;
	FILE: foreach $fname (grep {/\.pem$/} @flist) {
		# Check to see if certificates and/or CRLs present.
		my ($cert, $crl) = check_file($fname);
		if(!$cert && !$crl) {
			print STDERR "WARNING: $fname does not contain a certificate or CRL: skipping\n";
			next;
		}
		link_hash_cert($fname) if($cert);
		link_hash_crl($fname) if($crl);
	}
}

sub check_file {
	my ($is_cert, $is_crl) = (0,0);
	my $fname = $_[0];
	open IN, $fname;
	while(<IN>) {
		if(/^-----BEGIN (.*)-----/) {
			my $hdr = $1;
			if($hdr =~ /^(X509 |TRUSTED |)CERTIFICATE$/) {
				$is_cert = 1;
				last if($is_crl);
			} elsif($hdr eq "X509 CRL") {
				$is_crl = 1;
				last if($is_cert);
			}
		}
	}
	close IN;
	return ($is_cert, $is_crl);
}


# Link a certificate to its subject name hash value, each hash is of
# the form <hash>.<n> where n is an integer. If the hash value already exists
# then we need to up the value of n, unless its a duplicate in which
# case we skip the link. We check for duplicates by comparing the
# certificate fingerprints

sub link_hash_cert {
		my $fname = $_[0];
		$fname =~ s/'/'\\''/g;
		my ($hash, $fprint) = `"$openssl" x509 -hash -fingerprint -noout -in '$fname'`;
		chomp $hash;
		chomp $fprint;
		$fprint =~ s/^.*=//;
		$fprint =~ tr/://d;
		my $suffix = 0;
		# Search for an unused hash filename
		while(exists $hashlist{"$hash.$suffix"}) {
			# Hash matches: if fingerprint matches its a duplicate cert
			if($hashlist{"$hash.$suffix"} eq $fprint) {
				print STDERR "WARNING: Skipping duplicate certificate $fname\n";
				return;
			}
			$suffix++;
		}
		$hash .= ".$suffix";
		print "$fname => $hash\n";
		$symlink_exists=eval {symlink("",""); 1};
		if ($symlink_exists) {
			symlink $fname, $hash;
		} else {
			system ("cp", $fname, $hash);
		}
		$hashlist{$hash} = $fprint;
}

# Same as above except for a CRL. CRL links are of the form <hash>.r<n>

sub link_hash_crl {
		my $fname = $_[0];
		$fname =~ s/'/'\\''/g;
		my ($hash, $fprint) = `"$openssl" crl -hash -fingerprint -noout -in '$fname'`;
		chomp $hash;
		chomp $fprint;
		$fprint =~ s/^.*=//;
		$fprint =~ tr/://d;
		my $suffix = 0;
		# Search for an unused hash filename
		while(exists $hashlist{"$hash.r$suffix"}) {
			# Hash matches: if fingerprint matches its a duplicate cert
			if($hashlist{"$hash.r$suffix"} eq $fprint) {
				print STDERR "WARNING: Skipping duplicate CRL $fname\n";
				return;
			}
			$suffix++;
		}
		$hash .= ".r$suffix";
		print "$fname => $hash\n";
		$symlink_exists=eval {symlink("",""); 1};
		if ($symlink_exists) {
			symlink $fname, $hash;
		} else {
			system ("cp", $fname, $hash);
		}
		$hashlist{$hash} = $fprint;
}


#datagen
export JAVA_HOME=/ds/jdk1.7.0_25/
/ds/jdk1.7.0_25/bin/java com.relayhealth.datagen.Datagen $*

#decrypt_tpj

if [ ! -d "$DS_BASE_DIR" ]
  then
		echo "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory"
		exit 1
fi


for FILE in $*
do
echo "Decrypting $FILE"

echo $FILE | grep "[.]pgp$" > /dev/null

if [ $? != 0 ]
then
	echo "File appears not to be a pgp file"
	exit 1
fi

NEW_FILE=`echo $FILE | sed "s/[.]pgp//"`

#gpg --quiet --no-tty --no-permission-warning --passphrase-fd 0 --skip-verify --decrypt $FILE < /ds/gnupg/.pp > $NEW_FILE
cat /ds/gnupg/.pp | gpg --batch --quiet --no-tty --no-permission-warning --passphrase-fd 0 --decrypt --no $FILE > $NEW_FILE

RET=$?

echo $RET

if [ $RET != 0 ]
then
	echo "Error ($RET) decrypting $FILE "
else
  rm -f $FILE
fi 

done

exit 200


#df_report
#!/usr/bin/perl

eval 'exec /usr/bin/perl  -S $0 ${1+"$@"}'
    if 0; # not running under some shell

#
# Generic Script to run DF collector reports 
# author: David Liu
# date: 2/18/2010
#

#  Future enhancements
#
#   1) pass options specific to a report (constituent PDCs to Contractual reports)
#   2) show status of run (how far along it is) .. could be just how many files completed out of total
#   3) list dates associated to job_id / input_dir
#   4) show total file size for list_jobs
#   5) ? show time estimates for running a report
#   6) remove the need to have a wrapper script to set env variables for each feed
#   7) email

use strict;
use warnings;
use DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::Collector;
use DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::ReporterFactory;
use Data::Dumper;
use Getopt::Long;

# flush the buffer
$| = 1;

my $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s|.*/||g;
my $VERSION = $DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::VERSION;

my $JOB_ID;
my $REPORT_ID;
my $INPUT_DIR;
my $BEGIN_DATE;
my $END_DATE;
my $POST_DATE;
my $DISPLAY_WIDTH;
my $LOAD_TYPE;
my $EMAIL_TO;
my $REPORT_OPTIONS;

my $list_jobs = 0;
my $list_files = 0;
my $list_reports = 0;
my $list_dates = 0;

sub usage() {
  print "\n\n";
  print "========================================================================================\n";
  print "   Program:     $PGM                                            \n";
  print "   Version:     $VERSION                                        \n";
  print "   Description: This tool is used for reporting on data feeds   \n";
  print "                with collected data from the Data Feed Collector\n";
  print "========================================================================================\n";
  print "\n";
  print "    Usage: $PGM [-options] [file1 file2 file3 ... (optional)]\n";   
  print "\n";
  print "    TOOL OPTIONS                          DESCRIPTION \n";
  print "    -----------------------               ------------\n";
  print "    -list_jobs                            List JOB IDs in INPUT DIR\n";
  print "    -list_files                           List files in INPUT DIR, based on JOB ID\n";
  print "    -list_reports                         Display a list of reports\n";
#  print "    -list_dates                           Lists all dates for a given JOB ID\n";  
  print "\n";
  print "    REPORT OPTIONS                        DEFAULT\n";
  print "    -----------------------               --------------------\n";
  print "    -job_id                               N/A (required if not given a list of files)\n";
  print "    -report_id                            N/A (required)\n";  
  print "    -input_dir                            /temp/df_collector\n";
  print "    -load_type                            DMP\n";    
  print "    -begin_date                           N/A\n";
  print "    -end_date                             N/A\n";
  print "    -post_date                            N/A\n";  
  print "    -display_width                        80\n";
  print "    -email_to                             none (Separate multiple e-mails by commas or semicolons)\n";
  print "    -report_options                       none (ex. -report_options 'opt1=x,y,z;opt2=w;opt3=t,u')";
  print "\n\n";
  exit(1);
}


if(! eval { GetOptions('job_id=s'        => \$JOB_ID,
                       'report_id=s'     => \$REPORT_ID,
                       'input_dir=s'     => \$INPUT_DIR,                       
                       'begin_date=i'    => \$BEGIN_DATE,                       
                       'end_date=i'      => \$END_DATE,
                       'post_date=i'     => \$POST_DATE,
                       'display_width=i' => \$DISPLAY_WIDTH,
                       'load_type=s'     => \$LOAD_TYPE,
                       'email_to=s'      => \$EMAIL_TO,
                       'report_options=s'=> \$REPORT_OPTIONS,                       
                       'list_jobs'       => \$list_jobs,
                       'list_files',     => \$list_files,
                       'list_reports',   => \$list_reports,                       
                       'list_dates',     => \$list_dates                                 
                       );
           }
) {
    usage();
    exit(1);
}

if($PGM =~ /df_list_jobs/) {
  $list_jobs = 1;    
}
elsif($PGM =~ /df_list_files/) {
  $list_files = 1;  
}
elsif($PGM =~ /df_list_reports/) {
  $list_reports = 1;
}
elsif($PGM =~ /df_list_dates/) {
  $list_dates = 1;
}

my @collector_opts;
my @reporter_opts;

# no modes specified, mode is to report
if(($list_jobs | $list_files | $list_files | $list_reports) == 0) {
  
  # require a REPORT_ID
  if(! defined $REPORT_ID) {
    print STDERR "\n\nERROR: Param (report_id) is required!\n";
    usage();  
  }  
  
  # user specified to collect from files, JOB ID is inferred from files
  if(scalar (@ARGV) > 0) {
    push (@collector_opts, files => \@ARGV);     
  }
  # otherwise require a JOB_ID
  elsif(! defined $JOB_ID) {
    print STDERR "\n\nERROR: Param (job_id) is required\n";
    usage();
  }
  
  push (@reporter_opts, id => $REPORT_ID);
  
  if(defined $JOB_ID) {
    push (@collector_opts, job_id => $JOB_ID);
  }
  
  if(defined $INPUT_DIR) {
    push (@collector_opts, input_dir => $INPUT_DIR);
  } 
  
  if(defined $LOAD_TYPE) {
    push (@collector_opts, load_tpe => $LOAD_TYPE);
  }  
  
  if(defined $POST_DATE) {
    push (@reporter_opts, post_date => $POST_DATE);
  }
  
  if(defined $BEGIN_DATE) {
    push (@reporter_opts, begin_date => $BEGIN_DATE);
  }
  
  if(defined $END_DATE) {
    push (@reporter_opts, end_date => $END_DATE);
  }  
  
  if(defined $EMAIL_TO) {
    my @emails = split( /[,;]/, $EMAIL_TO);
    push (@reporter_opts, email_to => \@emails);   
  }
  
  if(defined $REPORT_OPTIONS) {
    my @options = split (/[;]/, $REPORT_OPTIONS);
    
    foreach my $option (@options) {
      my ($key, $value) = split(/[=]/, $option);
      if($value =~ /,/) {
        my @values = split(',',$value);
        push (@reporter_opts, $key => \@values);         
      }
      else {
        push (@reporter_opts, $key => $value); 
      }
    }
  }
  
  # test to see if reporter options are OK before running the report
  my @test_rpt_opts = @reporter_opts;
  my $col_obj = DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::Collector->new();
  push (@test_rpt_opts, collector => $col_obj);
  my $rpt_obj =  create_reporter(@test_rpt_opts);   
  
  print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "] Running $PGM on " . $ENV{HOSTNAME} . " with process ID " . $$ . "\n";  
  print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "] Collecting...\n";  
  $col_obj = DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::Collector->new(load_flag => 1, @collector_opts);
    
  push (@reporter_opts, collector => $col_obj); 
  
  print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "] Reporting...\n";

  $rpt_obj = create_reporter(@reporter_opts);
  my %opts = @reporter_opts;
  foreach my $key (sort keys %opts) {
    my $value = $opts{$key};
    print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "]   option: $key, value: $value\n";    
  }  
  $rpt_obj->execute();
  
  if(defined $DISPLAY_WIDTH) {
    $rpt_obj->print_text(width => $DISPLAY_WIDTH);
  }
  else {
    $rpt_obj->print_text();
  }
  
  print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "] Complete!\n";
  
}
# more than 1 mode specified 
elsif(($list_jobs ^ $list_files ^ $list_dates ^ $list_reports) != 1) {
  print STDERR "ERROR: Only one mode can be specified [list_jobs | list_files | list_reports | list_dates]\n";
  exit(1);  
}
# list jobs
elsif($list_jobs) {
  
  my %job_ids;
  if(! defined $INPUT_DIR) {
    $INPUT_DIR = '/temp/df_collector';
  }
  
  print STDERR "[" . scalar(localtime) . "] Inspecting dir '$INPUT_DIR' for files...\n";
  
  if(! opendir(DIR,$INPUT_DIR) ) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot open input directory '$INPUT_DIR'";
    exit(1);   
  }

  foreach my $file (readdir(DIR)) {;
    if($file =~ /^([A-Z0-9_\-]+)_\d{8}(?:-\d{8})?_.*$/) {
      $job_ids{$1}++; 
    }
  }
  
  closedir DIR;
  
  my $format = "%-25.25s %-25.25s\n";
  
  print "\n\n";
  printf $format, "Job ID", "Number of files";
  print "=" x 80 . "\n";
  foreach my $id (sort { $job_ids{$b} <=> $job_ids{$a}} keys %job_ids) {
    printf $format, $id, $job_ids{$id};             
  }
  print "\n\n";  
  
}
# list files
elsif($list_files) {
  
  if(defined $INPUT_DIR) {
    push @collector_opts, input_dir => $INPUT_DIR;
  }
  
  if(! defined $JOB_ID) {
    print STDERR "\n\nERROR: Param (job_id) is required\n";
    usage();
  }
  
  push (@collector_opts, job_id => $JOB_ID);    
  
  my $obj = DS::DataFeed::Analyzer::Collector->new(@collector_opts);
  foreach my $f ($obj->list_files) {
    print "$f\n";
  }
}
# list reports
elsif($list_reports) {
  list_reporters();
}
# list dates
elsif($list_dates) {
  
}

# should not get here
else {
  print STDERR "ERROR: UNKNOWN ERROR OCCURRED";
  exit(1);
}

#dimension_load3
#!/usr/bin/perl

# v3.0 - 5/25/2012 - Added calls for pre_load and post_load methods, and added parallel option for load method call.

use strict;
use warnings;

use DateTime;
use File::Basename;
use DS::Dimension;
use Getopt::Long;
use Data::Dumper;
use Proc::ProcessTable;
$Data::Dumper::Useqq = 1;

our $DIM_CONSTANTS;

$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/address';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'FILEMASK'}	= '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medcontrol';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medicaid';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
#$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ZIPCODE'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_source/dimensions/zipcode';


our $mode;
our $prog;
our $ret;
our $debug;
our $dim_maint_obj;
our $dim_obj;

sub file_exists($) {
  my($input_file) = shift;

  if (-f $input_file ||	-l $input_file)	{
    return 1;
  } elsif (system("ls $input_file > /dev/null 2>&1") !=	0) {
    return 0;
  } else {
    return 1;
  }
}


sub Usage() {
	print "\n";
	print "USAGE:\n";
	print "  dimension_maint  [-options] filename\n";
	print "  dimension_load   [-options] filename\n";
	print "  dimension_list   [-options]\n";
	print "  dimension_report [-options]\n";
	print "\n";

	print "OPTIONS:\n";
	print "  -load                       Load the file to the appropriate dimension table\n";
	print "  -num-split-files #          Split input file into # pieces and load in parallel\n";
	print "  -prun2-opts '-r hosts ...'  Specify prun2 options when using -num-split-files\n";
	print "  -resume                     Finish prior -load attempt\n";
	print "  -move                       Force move of input file to data_sources dest dir after successful load\n";
	print "  -dim                        Indicates the Dimension package to	use\n";
	print "  -list                       List the availiable packages\n";
	print "  -dir                        Specify the directory to move the file after loading (only	used with load)\n";
	print "\n";
}

our $report = 0;
our $load = 0;
our $list = 0;
our $stats = 0;
our ($dimension, $post_date, $base_dir, $file_mask);

$prog =	$0;

if ($prog =~ /dimension_list/) {
	$list =	1;
	$mode =	"LIST";
} elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_report/) {
	$report	= 1;
	$mode =	"REPORT";
} elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_load/) {
	$load =	1;
	$mode =	"LOAD";
} else {
	$mode =	"MAINT";
}

my $child_load = 0;
my $prun2_opts = '-m 3';
my $num_split_files;
my $resume = 0;
my $move = 0;

$ret = GetOptions(  "debug", \$debug,
					"load",	\$load,
					"-num-split-files=s",	\$num_split_files,
					"-prun2-opts=s",	\$prun2_opts,
					"report", \$report,
					"stats", \$stats,
					"list",	\$list,
					"dim|d=s", \$dimension,
					"help|h", sub {	Usage()	; exit(0) },
					"post_date|p=s", \$post_date,
					"dir=s", \$base_dir,
					"filemask=s",\$file_mask,
					"child-load",	\$child_load,
					"move",	\$move,
					"resume",	\$resume,
					);

if (! $ret)
{
	Usage();
	exit(1);
}

if (defined($post_date))
{
		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($post_date))
		{
			print STDERR "$prog: The specified date	of \"$post_date\" is invalid\n";
			print STDERR "$prog: Use the format YYYYMMDD and/or Check the validity of the date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
}

if ($list)
{
	if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		$dimension = shift @ARGV;
	}

	if ($dimension)
	{
		$dim_maint_obj=	&get_dimension($dimension);
	}
	else
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->list;

	exit(0);
}
elsif ($report)
{
	$dimension = shift @ARGV if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0);

	if ($dimension) {
		$dim_maint_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
	} else {
		$dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->report;

	exit(0);

} elsif ($load) {

	die "ERROR: No dimension package indicated.\nRerun command with -h for help\n" if (! defined $dimension);
	die "ERROR: Cannot use -child-load and -num-split-files options together\n" if (defined($num_split_files) && $child_load);

	my ($do_parent, $do_child);

	if (defined($num_split_files)) {
		$do_parent = 1;
		$do_child = 0;
	} elsif ($child_load) {
		$do_parent = 0;
		$do_child = 1;
	} else {
		$do_parent = 1;
		$do_child = 1;
	}

		#print "\n\t*** DEBUG ***\n";
		#print "\t\t\$num_split_files = [$num_split_files]\n";
		#print "\t\t\$prun2_opts = [$prun2_opts]\n";
		#print "\t\t\@ARGV = [@ARGV]\n";
		#print "\n";
		#exit 1;

	die "ERROR: No files specified for loading\n" if (! @ARGV);
	die "ERROR: Only 1 file can be specified\n" if(scalar(@ARGV) >	1);
	die "ERROR: Ouput directory '$base_dir' does not exist!\n" if ($do_parent && $base_dir && ! (-e $base_dir && -d $base_dir));

	####################################################################################################

	my $input_file = $ARGV[0];
	die "ERROR: File '$input_file' does not exist!\n" if (! -f $input_file);

	$post_date = get_post_date_from_file($input_file) if (! defined($post_date));

	if ($do_parent) {
		my $t = new Proc::ProcessTable;

    foreach my $p ( @{$t->table} ){
      if(($p->pid != $$) && ($p->cmndline =~ /$input_file/) && ($p->cmndline =~ m!/usr/bin/perl/!)) {
        die "ERROR: Duplicate process already running!\n";
      }
    }
	}

	$dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);

	if ($do_parent && $dim_obj->can('pre_load')) {
		die "ERROR: pre_load() method failed!\n" if (! $dim_obj->pre_load(POST_DATE => $post_date, FILE => $input_file, resume => $resume));
	}

	if ($do_child) {
		die "ERROR: load() method failed!\n" if (! $dim_obj->load(POST_DATE => $post_date, FILE => $input_file));
		exit(0) if (! $do_parent);
	}

	if (defined($num_split_files)) {
		my $command = "split_run -num-files $num_split_files ";
		$command .= "-resume " if ($resume);
		$command .= "-prun2-opts '$prun2_opts' " if (defined($prun2_opts));
		$command .= "-command '$prog -dim $dimension -child-load ' $input_file";

		print "$command\n";

		die "ERROR: Parent dimension load could not successfully run all child work units!\n" if (system($command) != 0);
	}

	if ($do_parent && $dim_obj->can('post_load')) {
		die "ERROR: post_load() method failed!\n" if (! $dim_obj->post_load(POST_DATE => $post_date, FILE => $input_file));
	}

	# Rename/Move after loading

		my ($name, $path, $suff) = File::Basename::fileparse($input_file);
		my $cps_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/cps/";
		my $tandem_source_dir =	"/ds/data_sources/incoming/tandem/";
		my $pscbr_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/prescriber/";
		my $out_dir = $base_dir;

		if($move || ($path eq $cps_source_dir) || ($path	eq $tandem_source_dir) || ($path eq $pscbr_source_dir))	{ # move files only if they haven't been moved from the	source directory

			if (($name =~ /^(.*MDCAID[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~	/^(.*ADDR[0-9]{4}.*)$/)	||
			       ($name =~ /^(medctrl_(\d){8}\.dat)$/) ||	($name =~ /^(.*BIN[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PIDS[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~ /^(.*GRP[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PHGP[0-9]{4}.*)$/)) {

				my $new_full_name = "$1.gz";
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$new_full_name = $out_dir . $new_full_name;

				$ret = system("gzip -c '$input_file' > $new_full_name");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_full_name) {
						unlink($input_file);
					}
				} else {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip '$input_file' to $new_full_name\n";
					unlink($new_full_name);
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^WA\d{6}\.zip$/)) {

				$out_dir = "$base_dir/active/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $input_file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$input_file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^MAR\d{6}\.zip$/)) {
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/retired/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $input_file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$input_file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (    ($name =~ /^\d{8}_NPI\.csv\.gz$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_csr\.txt\.gz$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{4}EXCL\.DBF$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{4}REIN\.DBF$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_surescripts\.txt\.zip$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_AI_(PHY|DDS)\.txt\.gz$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_STLICENSE_FL\.txt\.gz$/)
						 ) {
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $input_file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$input_file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}					

		}

	exit(0);
}
elsif($stats) {

	# Gets stats on	existing or potential dimensions
	# If a dimension is not	specified, it will get stats on	files located in the dir with filemask
	# If a dimension is specified, it will get stats on existing dimensions

	# Stats	returned:
	#	a) Number of files scanned
	#	b) Average number of records per file
	#   c) Average number of characters per	record

	my @stats = (0,0,0);

	if(not defined $dimension) {
		if((not	defined	$base_dir) or (not defined $file_mask))	{
			&Usage();
			exit(0);
		}

		&get_stats($base_dir, $file_mask, \@stats);

	}
	else {
		my $dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
		my $base_dir = $DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'BASEDIR'};
		my $file_mask =	$DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'FILEMASK'};

		&get_stats($base_dir,$file_mask	, \@stats);

	}

	if($stats[0] &&	$stats[1] && $stats[2])	{
		print "Number of files:	$stats[0]\n";
		print "Avg. num	of records per file: " . $stats[1]/$stats[0] ."\n";
		print "Avg. chars per line: " .	$stats[2]/$stats[1] . "\n";
		exit(0);
	}
}

sub get_stats {

	my $dir	= shift;
	my $mask = shift; #mask	is a regex expression to match files in	that directory
	my $stats_ref =	shift;
	opendir	DH, $dir or die	"ERROR:	Could not open directory '$dir'\n";
	foreach	(readdir(DH)) {
		next if	$_ =~ /^\./;
		if ( -d	"$dir/$_" ) {
			&get_stats("$dir/$_", $mask, $stats_ref);
		}
		else {
			if ($_ =~ /$mask/) {
				open (IN,"read_file '$dir/$_' |") || die "Cannot open file (via	readfile) \"$_\" due to	$!";
				print "collecting stats: $_\n";
				$stats_ref->[0]++;

				while(<IN>) {
					$stats_ref->[1]+=1;
					$stats_ref->[2]+=length($_) - 1;
				}
				close IN;
#print "files: $stats_ref->[0],	recs: $stats_ref->[1], chars: $stats_ref->[2]\n";
			}
		}
	}
	close DH;
}

sub get_dimension {
	my $dimension =	shift;
	my $dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	my $dimension_obj = $dim_maint_obj->new_dimension(DIM_ID => $dimension);
	if(!$dimension_obj) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to aquire Dimension	Maint object - aborting\n";
		exit(1);
	}
	else {
		return $dimension_obj;
	}
}

sub get_post_date_from_file {
	my $file = shift;

	if(scalar(@_) >	1)
	{
		printf "WARNING: Cannot	generate post date from	multiple files\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my ($cc, $yy, $mm, $dd);
	my ($name, $path, $suffix) = File::Basename::fileparse($file);
	my $stat_date =	&date_from_stat($file);
	my $file_date;

	# name could be	CCYYMMDD, YYMMDD, MMDD,	MM

	if($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{8}).*$/)			# CCYYMMDD?
	{
		my $tmp_date = $1;
		if($stat_date !~ /^$tmp_date$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$1'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($tmp_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$tmp_date' in file '$file' is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $tmp_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# YYMMDD?
	{
		$yy = $1;
		$mm = $2;
		$dd = $3;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,2) . $yy . $mm	. $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{2})($yy)($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";			
			#print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming date '$stat_date'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			print $file_date ."\n";
			return $file_date;
			#return $stat_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MMDD?
	{
		$mm = $1;
		$dd = $2;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,4)  . $mm . $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			#print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$stat_date'\n";
		}


		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($stat_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$stat_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $stat_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MM?
	{
		$mm = $1;

		$file_date = DS::Dimension::end_of_month(substr($stat_date,0,4) .	$mm);

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)([0-9]{2})$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $file_date;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		print STDERR "WARNING: No date in filename, using date from stat '$stat_date'\n";
		return $stat_date;
	}

}

sub date_from_stat($) {

  my $file = shift;
	my ($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$size,$atime,$mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks)	= stat $file;
	my $dt = DateTime->from_epoch( epoch =>	$mtime,	time_zone  => 'local' );
	my $date = sprintf ("%04d%02d%02d", $dt->year, $dt->month, $dt->day);
	return $date;
}

if(! shift @ARGV) {
	&Usage();
}


#dimension_maint
#!/usr/bin/perl

use strict;
use warnings;
use DateTime;
use File::Basename;
use BLUELITE::Dimension;
use Getopt::Long;
use Data::Dumper;
use Proc::ProcessTable;
$Data::Dumper::Useqq = 1;

our $DIM_CONSTANTS;

$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/address';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'FILEMASK'}	= '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medcontrol';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medicaid';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'CONTRACTUAL'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/pal/lookup_data/contract_exclusions';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'CONTRACTUAL'}{'FILEMASK'} = '(InclExcl)|([.]PX)|([.]IL)';
#$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ZIPCODE'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_source/dimensions/zipcode';


our $mode;
our $prog;
our $ret;
our $debug;
our $dim_maint_obj;
our $dim_obj;
our @filenames;

sub file_exists($) {
  my($input_file) = shift;

  if (-f $input_file ||	-l $input_file)	{
    return 1;
  } elsif (system("ls $input_file > /dev/null 2>&1") !=	0) {
    return 0;
  } else {
    return 1;
  }
}


sub Usage()
{
	print "\n";
	print "USAGE:\n";
	print "	      dimension_maint [	options	] [ filename ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_load [ options ] [ filename ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_list [ options ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_report [ options ]\n";
	print "\n";

	print "OPTIONS:\n";
	print "	       -list	     List the availiable packages\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -dim	     Indicates the Dimension package to	use\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -load	     Do	not register the data source as	an available data source to the	BLUELITE\n";
	print "			     database\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -dir	     Specify the directory to move the file after loading (only	used with load)\n";
	print "\n";

}

our ($method, $option);
our $report = 0;
our $load = 0;
our $list = 0;
our $stats = 0;
our $dimension;
our $post_date;
our $base_dir;
our $file_mask;

	$prog =	$0;

	if ($prog =~ /dimension_list/)
	{
		$list =	1;
		$mode =	"LIST";
	}
	elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_report/)
	{
		$report	= 1;
		$mode =	"REPORT";
	}
	elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_load/)
	{
		$load =	1;
		$mode =	"LOAD";
	}
	else
	{
		$mode =	"MAINT";
	}



$ret = GetOptions(  "debug", \$debug,
					"load",	\$load,
					"report", \$report,
					"stats", \$stats,
					"list",	\$list,
					"dim|d=s", \$dimension,
					"help|h", sub {	Usage()	; exit(0) },
					"post_date|p=s", \$post_date,
					"dir=s", \$base_dir,
					"filemask=s",\$file_mask
					);

if (! $ret)
{
	Usage();
	exit(1);
}

if (defined($post_date))
{
		if (! BLUELITE::Dimension::is_date_valid($post_date))
		{
			print STDERR "$prog: The specified date	of \"$post_date\" is invalid\n";
			print STDERR "$prog: Use the format YYYYMMDD and/or Check the validity of the date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
}

if ($list)
{
	if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		$dimension = shift @ARGV;
	}

	if ($dimension)
	{
		$dim_maint_obj=	&get_dimension($dimension);
	}
	else
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = BLUELITE::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->list;

	exit(0);
}
elsif ($report)
{
	if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		$dimension = shift @ARGV;
	}

	if ($dimension)
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
	}
	else
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = BLUELITE::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->report;

	exit(0);
}
elsif ($load)
{
	if(not defined $dimension) {
		print STDERR "No dimension package indicated.\nRerun command with -h for help\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if(($base_dir) && (! (-e $base_dir && -d $base_dir)) ) {
		print STDERR "Ouput directory '$base_dir' does not exist!\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if(scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		@filenames = @ARGV;

		### Only allow 1 file to be loaded (remove this	section	of code	if you want to allow multiple files)

		if(scalar(@filenames) >	1) {
			print "WARNING:	Loading	only the first file specified\n";
			@filenames = $ARGV[0];
		}
		####################################################################################################

		foreach	(@filenames) {
			if(not -f $_) {
				print STDERR "Unable to	locate file '$_'\n";
				exit (1);
			}
		}

		if(not defined $post_date)
		{
			$post_date = get_post_date_from_file(@filenames);
		}
	}
	else
	{
		print STDERR "No files specified for loading\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	my $t = new Proc::ProcessTable;

    foreach my $p ( @{$t->table} ){
      if(($p->pid != $$) && ($p->cmndline =~ /$filenames[0]/) && ($p->cmndline =~ m!/usr/bin/perl/!)) {
        print STDERR "Duplicate process already running!\n";
        exit(1);
      }
    }


	$dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
	$dim_obj->load(POST_DATE => $post_date,	FILES => \@filenames);

	# Rename/Move after loading

	foreach	(@filenames) {

		my $file = $_;
		my ($name, $path, $suff) = File::Basename::fileparse($file);
		my $cps_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/cps/";
		my $tandem_source_dir =	"/ds/data_sources/incoming/tandem/";
		my $pscbr_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/prescriber/";
		my $out_dir = $base_dir;

		if(($path eq $cps_source_dir) || ($path	eq $tandem_source_dir) || ($path eq $pscbr_source_dir))	{ # move files only if they haven't been moved from the	source directory

			if ($name =~ /^\$?([^.]+)[.](DOWNLOAD|HCPSDNLD)[.]([^0-9]+)([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})[^0-9]*$/i){
				my ($prefix, $root, $suffix, $yy, $mm, $dd) = ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6);
				my $new_full_name = "$out_dir/"	. "${prefix}.${root}.${suffix}${yy}${mm}${dd}.gz";

				$ret = system("gzip -c '$file' > $new_full_name");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_full_name) {
						unlink($file);
					}
				} else {

					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip '$file' to $new_full_name\n";
					unlink($new_full_name);
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^(.*MDCAID[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~	/^(.*ADDR[0-9]{4}.*)$/)	||
			       ($name =~ /^(medctrl_(\d){8}\.dat)$/) ||	($name =~ /^(.*BIN[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PIDS[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~ /^(.*GRP[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PHGP[0-9]{4}.*)$/)) {

				my $new_full_name = "$1.gz";
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$new_full_name = $out_dir . $new_full_name;

				$ret = system("gzip -c '$file' > $new_full_name");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_full_name) {
						unlink($file);
					}
				} else {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip '$file' to $new_full_name\n";
					unlink($new_full_name);
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^WA\d{6}\.zip$/)) {

				$out_dir = "$base_dir/active/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^MAR\d{6}\.zip$/)) {
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/retired/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}

		}
	}
	exit(0);
}
elsif($stats) {

	# Gets stats on	existing or potential dimensions
	# If a dimension is not	specified, it will get stats on	files located in the dir with filemask
	# If a dimension is specified, it will get stats on existing dimensions

	# Stats	returned:
	#	a) Number of files scanned
	#	b) Average number of records per file
	#   c) Average number of characters per	record

	my @stats = (0,0,0);

	if(not defined $dimension) {
		if((not	defined	$base_dir) or (not defined $file_mask))	{
			&Usage();
			exit(0);
		}

		&get_stats($base_dir, $file_mask, \@stats);

	}
	else {
		my $dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
		my $base_dir = $DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'BASEDIR'};
		my $file_mask =	$DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'FILEMASK'};

		&get_stats($base_dir,$file_mask	, \@stats);

	}

	if($stats[0] &&	$stats[1] && $stats[2])	{
		print "Number of files:	$stats[0]\n";
		print "Avg. num	of records per file: " . $stats[1]/$stats[0] ."\n";
		print "Avg. chars per line: " .	$stats[2]/$stats[1] . "\n";
		exit(0);
	}
}

sub get_stats {

	my $dir	= shift;
	my $mask = shift; #mask	is a regex expression to match files in	that directory
	my $stats_ref =	shift;
	opendir	DH, $dir or die	"ERROR:	Could not open directory '$dir'\n";
	foreach	(readdir(DH)) {
		next if	$_ =~ /^\./;
		if ( -d	"$dir/$_" ) {
			&get_stats("$dir/$_", $mask, $stats_ref);
		}
		else {
			if ($_ =~ /$mask/) {
				open (IN,"read_file '$dir/$_' |") || die "Cannot open file (via	readfile) \"$_\" due to	$!";
				print "collecting stats: $_\n";
				$stats_ref->[0]++;

				while(<IN>) {
					$stats_ref->[1]+=1;
					$stats_ref->[2]+=length($_) - 1;
				}
				close IN;
#print "files: $stats_ref->[0],	recs: $stats_ref->[1], chars: $stats_ref->[2]\n";
			}
		}
	}
	close DH;
}

sub get_dimension {
	my $dimension =	shift;
	my $dim_maint_obj = BLUELITE::Dimension->new();
	my $dimension_obj = $dim_maint_obj->new_dimension(DIM_ID => $dimension);
	if(!$dimension_obj) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to aquire Dimension	Maint object - aborting\n";
		exit(1);
	}
	else {
		return $dimension_obj;
	}
}

sub get_post_date_from_file {
	my $file = shift;

	if(scalar(@_) >	1)
	{
		printf "WARNING: Cannot	generate post date from	multiple files\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my ($cc, $yy, $mm, $dd);
	my ($name, $path, $suffix) = File::Basename::fileparse($file);
	my $stat_date =	&date_from_stat($file);
	my $file_date;

	# name could be	CCYYMMDD, YYMMDD, MMDD,	MM

	if($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{8}).*$/)			# CCYYMMDD?
	{
		my $tmp_date = $1;
		if($stat_date !~ /^$tmp_date$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$1'\n";
		}

		if (! BLUELITE::Dimension::is_date_valid($tmp_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$tmp_date' in file '$file' is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $tmp_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# YYMMDD?
	{
		$yy = $1;
		$mm = $2;
		$dd = $3;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,2) . $yy . $mm	. $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{2})($yy)($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
		}

		if (! BLUELITE::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $file_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MMDD?
	{
		$mm = $1;
		$dd = $2;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,4)  . $mm . $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
		}

		if (! BLUELITE::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $file_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MM?
	{
		$mm = $1;

		$file_date = BLUELITE::Dimension::end_of_month(substr($stat_date,0,4) .	$mm);

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)([0-9]{2})$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
		}

		if (! BLUELITE::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $file_date;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		print STDERR "WARNING: No date in filename, using date from stat '$stat_date'\n";
		return $stat_date;
	}

}

sub date_from_stat($) {

  my $file = shift;
	my ($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$size,$atime,$mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks)	= stat $file;
	my $dt = DateTime->from_epoch( epoch =>	$mtime,	time_zone  => 'local' );
	my $date = sprintf ("%04d%02d%02d", $dt->year, $dt->month, $dt->day);
	return $date;
}

if(! shift @ARGV) {
	&Usage();
}


#dimension_maint2
#!/usr/bin/perl

use strict;
use warnings;
use DateTime;
use File::Basename;
use DS::Dimension;
use Getopt::Long;
use Data::Dumper;
use Proc::ProcessTable;
$Data::Dumper::Useqq = 1;

our $DIM_CONSTANTS;

$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/address';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ADDRESS'}{'FILEMASK'}	= '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medcontrol';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDCONTROL'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_sources/dimensions/medicaid';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'MEDICAID'}{'FILEMASK'} = '.*';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'CONTRACTUAL'}{'BASEDIR'} = '/ds/pal/lookup_data/contract_exclusions';
$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'CONTRACTUAL'}{'FILEMASK'} = '(InclExcl)|([.]PX)|([.]IL)';
#$DIM_CONSTANTS->{'ZIPCODE'}{'BASEDIR'}	= '/ds/data_source/dimensions/zipcode';


our $mode;
our $prog;
our $ret;
our $debug;
our $dim_maint_obj;
our $dim_obj;
our @filenames;

sub file_exists($) {
  my($input_file) = shift;

  if (-f $input_file ||	-l $input_file)	{
    return 1;
  } elsif (system("ls $input_file > /dev/null 2>&1") !=	0) {
    return 0;
  } else {
    return 1;
  }
}


sub Usage()
{
	print "\n";
	print "USAGE:\n";
	print "	      dimension_maint [	options	] [ filename ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_load [ options ] [ filename ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_list [ options ]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	      dimension_report [ options ]\n";
	print "\n";

	print "OPTIONS:\n";
	print "	       -list	     List the availiable packages\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -dim	     Indicates the Dimension package to	use\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -load	     Do	not register the data source as	an available data source to the	BLUELITE\n";
	print "			     database\n";
	print "\n";
	print "	       -dir	     Specify the directory to move the file after loading (only	used with load)\n";
	print "\n";

}

our ($method, $option);
our $report = 0;
our $load = 0;
our $list = 0;
our $stats = 0;
our $dimension;
our $post_date;
our $base_dir;
our $file_mask;

	$prog =	$0;

	if ($prog =~ /dimension_list2/)
	{
		$list =	1;
		$mode =	"LIST";
	}
	elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_report2/)
	{
		$report	= 1;
		$mode =	"REPORT";
	}
	elsif ($prog =~	/dimension_load2/)
	{
		$load =	1;
		$mode =	"LOAD";
	}
	else
	{
		$mode =	"MAINT";
	}



$ret = GetOptions(  "debug", \$debug,
					"load",	\$load,
					"report", \$report,
					"stats", \$stats,
					"list",	\$list,
					"dim|d=s", \$dimension,
					"help|h", sub {	Usage()	; exit(0) },
					"post_date|p=s", \$post_date,
					"dir=s", \$base_dir,
					"filemask=s",\$file_mask
					);

if (! $ret)
{
	Usage();
	exit(1);
}

if (defined($post_date))
{
		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($post_date))
		{
			print STDERR "$prog: The specified date	of \"$post_date\" is invalid\n";
			print STDERR "$prog: Use the format YYYYMMDD and/or Check the validity of the date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
}

if ($list)
{
	if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		$dimension = shift @ARGV;
	}

	if ($dimension)
	{
		$dim_maint_obj=	&get_dimension($dimension);
	}
	else
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->list;

	exit(0);
}
elsif ($report)
{
	if (scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		$dimension = shift @ARGV;
	}

	if ($dimension)
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
	}
	else
	{
		$dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	}

	$dim_maint_obj->report;

	exit(0);
}
elsif ($load)
{
	if(not defined $dimension) {
		print STDERR "No dimension package indicated.\nRerun command with -h for help\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if(($base_dir) && (! (-e $base_dir && -d $base_dir)) ) {
		print STDERR "Ouput directory '$base_dir' does not exist!\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if(scalar(@ARGV) != 0)
	{
		@filenames = @ARGV;

		### Only allow 1 file to be loaded (remove this	section	of code	if you want to allow multiple files)

		if(scalar(@filenames) >	1) {
			print "WARNING:	Loading	only the first file specified\n";
			@filenames = $ARGV[0];
		}
		####################################################################################################

		foreach	(@filenames) {
			if(not -f $_) {
				print STDERR "Unable to	locate file '$_'\n";
				exit (1);
			}
		}

		if(not defined $post_date)
		{
			$post_date = get_post_date_from_file(@filenames);
		}
	}
	else
	{
		print STDERR "No files specified for loading\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	my $t = new Proc::ProcessTable;

    foreach my $p ( @{$t->table} ){
      if(($p->pid != $$) && ($p->cmndline =~ /$filenames[0]/) && ($p->cmndline =~ m!/usr/bin/perl/!)) {
        print STDERR "Duplicate process already running!\n";
        exit(1);
      }
    }

	$dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
	$dim_obj->load(POST_DATE => $post_date,	FILES => \@filenames);

	# Rename/Move after loading
	foreach	(@filenames) {

		my $file = $_;
		my ($name, $path, $suff) = File::Basename::fileparse($file);
		my $cps_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/cps/";
		my $tandem_source_dir =	"/ds/data_sources/incoming/tandem/";
		my $pscbr_source_dir = "/ds/data_sources/incoming/prescriber/";
		my $out_dir = $base_dir;

		if(($path eq $cps_source_dir) || ($path	eq $tandem_source_dir) || ($path eq $pscbr_source_dir))	{ # move files only if they haven't been moved from the	source directory

			if ($name =~ /^\$?([^.]+)[.](DOWNLOAD|HCPSDNLD)[.]([^0-9]+)([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})[^0-9]*$/i){
				my ($prefix, $root, $suffix, $yy, $mm, $dd) = ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6);
				my $new_full_name = "$out_dir/"	. "${prefix}.${root}.${suffix}${yy}${mm}${dd}.gz";

				$ret = system("gzip -c '$file' > $new_full_name");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_full_name) {
						unlink($file);
					}
				} else {

					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip '$file' to $new_full_name\n";
					unlink($new_full_name);
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^(.*MDCAID[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~	/^(.*ADDR[0-9]{4}.*)$/)	||
			       ($name =~ /^(medctrl_(\d){8}\.dat)$/) ||	($name =~ /^(.*BIN[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PIDS[0-9]{4}.*)$/) || ($name =~ /^(.*GRP[0-9]{4}.*)$/) ||
			       ($name =~ /^(.*PHGP[0-9]{4}.*)$/)) {

				my $new_full_name = "$1.gz";
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$new_full_name = $out_dir . $new_full_name;

				$ret = system("gzip -c '$file' > $new_full_name");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_full_name) {
						unlink($file);
					}
				} else {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip '$file' to $new_full_name\n";
					unlink($new_full_name);
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^WA\d{6}\.zip$/)) {

				$out_dir = "$base_dir/active/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (($name =~ /^MAR\d{6}\.zip$/)) {
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/retired/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}
			elsif (    ($name =~ /^\d{8}_NPI\.csv\.gz$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_csr\.txt\.gz$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{4}EXCL\.DBF$/) 
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{4}REIN\.DBF$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_surescripts\.txt\.zip$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_AI_(PHY|DDS)\.txt\.gz$/)
							|| ($name =~ /^\d{8}_STLICENSE_FL\.txt\.gz$/)
						 ) {
				$out_dir = "$base_dir/". substr($post_date,0,4)	. "/";

				if(! -e	$out_dir) {
					$ret = system("mkdir $out_dir");
					$ret = $ret >> 8;
					if($ret	!= 0) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create dir $out_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}

				$ret = system("mv $file $out_dir");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;
				if ($ret != 0) {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to mv '$file' to $out_dir\n";
					exit(1);
				}
			}					

		}
	}
	exit(0);
}
elsif($stats) {

	# Gets stats on	existing or potential dimensions
	# If a dimension is not	specified, it will get stats on	files located in the dir with filemask
	# If a dimension is specified, it will get stats on existing dimensions

	# Stats	returned:
	#	a) Number of files scanned
	#	b) Average number of records per file
	#   c) Average number of characters per	record

	my @stats = (0,0,0);

	if(not defined $dimension) {
		if((not	defined	$base_dir) or (not defined $file_mask))	{
			&Usage();
			exit(0);
		}

		&get_stats($base_dir, $file_mask, \@stats);

	}
	else {
		my $dim_obj = &get_dimension($dimension);
		my $base_dir = $DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'BASEDIR'};
		my $file_mask =	$DIM_CONSTANTS->{uc($dimension)}{'FILEMASK'};

		&get_stats($base_dir,$file_mask	, \@stats);

	}

	if($stats[0] &&	$stats[1] && $stats[2])	{
		print "Number of files:	$stats[0]\n";
		print "Avg. num	of records per file: " . $stats[1]/$stats[0] ."\n";
		print "Avg. chars per line: " .	$stats[2]/$stats[1] . "\n";
		exit(0);
	}
}

sub get_stats {

	my $dir	= shift;
	my $mask = shift; #mask	is a regex expression to match files in	that directory
	my $stats_ref =	shift;
	opendir	DH, $dir or die	"ERROR:	Could not open directory '$dir'\n";
	foreach	(readdir(DH)) {
		next if	$_ =~ /^\./;
		if ( -d	"$dir/$_" ) {
			&get_stats("$dir/$_", $mask, $stats_ref);
		}
		else {
			if ($_ =~ /$mask/) {
				open (IN,"read_file '$dir/$_' |") || die "Cannot open file (via	readfile) \"$_\" due to	$!";
				print "collecting stats: $_\n";
				$stats_ref->[0]++;

				while(<IN>) {
					$stats_ref->[1]+=1;
					$stats_ref->[2]+=length($_) - 1;
				}
				close IN;
#print "files: $stats_ref->[0],	recs: $stats_ref->[1], chars: $stats_ref->[2]\n";
			}
		}
	}
	close DH;
}

sub get_dimension {
	my $dimension =	shift;
	my $dim_maint_obj = DS::Dimension->new();
	my $dimension_obj = $dim_maint_obj->new_dimension(DIM_ID => $dimension);
	if(!$dimension_obj) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to aquire Dimension	Maint object - aborting\n";
		exit(1);
	}
	else {
		return $dimension_obj;
	}
}

sub get_post_date_from_file {
	my $file = shift;

	if(scalar(@_) >	1)
	{
		printf "WARNING: Cannot	generate post date from	multiple files\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my ($cc, $yy, $mm, $dd);
	my ($name, $path, $suffix) = File::Basename::fileparse($file);
	my $stat_date =	&date_from_stat($file);
	my $file_date;

	# name could be	CCYYMMDD, YYMMDD, MMDD,	MM

	if($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{8}).*$/)			# CCYYMMDD?
	{
		my $tmp_date = $1;
		if($stat_date !~ /^$tmp_date$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$1'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($tmp_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$tmp_date' in file '$file' is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $tmp_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# YYMMDD?
	{
		$yy = $1;
		$mm = $2;
		$dd = $3;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,2) . $yy . $mm	. $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{2})($yy)($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";			
			#print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming date '$stat_date'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			print $file_date ."\n";
			return $file_date;
			#return $stat_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2})([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MMDD?
	{
		$mm = $1;
		$dd = $2;

		$file_date = substr($stat_date,0,4)  . $mm . $dd;

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)($dd)$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			#print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$stat_date'\n";
		}


		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($stat_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$stat_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $stat_date;
		}
	}
	elsif($name =~ /^.*([0-9]{2}).*$/)	# MM?
	{
		$mm = $1;

		$file_date = DS::Dimension::end_of_month(substr($stat_date,0,4) .	$mm);

		if($stat_date !~ /^([0-9]{4})($mm)([0-9]{2})$/)
		{
			print STDERR "WARNING: Date in filename	'$name'	does not match stat date '$stat_date'\n";
			print STDERR "WARNING: Assuming	date '$file_date'\n";
		}

		if (! DS::Dimension::is_date_valid($file_date))
		{
			print STDERR "ERROR: Date '$file_date' in file is an invalid date\n";
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		{
			return $file_date;
		}
	}
	else
	{
		print STDERR "WARNING: No date in filename, using date from stat '$stat_date'\n";
		return $stat_date;
	}

}

sub date_from_stat($) {

  my $file = shift;
	my ($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$size,$atime,$mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks)	= stat $file;
	my $dt = DateTime->from_epoch( epoch =>	$mtime,	time_zone  => 'local' );
	my $date = sprintf ("%04d%02d%02d", $dt->year, $dt->month, $dt->day);
	return $date;
}

if(! shift @ARGV) {
	&Usage();
}


#disk_space.sh
#!/bin/sh
# disk_space.sh
# Checks all directories on dsgrid02a and reports if they are over 90%
# B.Oliver 7-22-22

df -H | grep -vE '^Filesystem|tmpfs|cdrom' | awk '{ print $5 " " $6 }' | while read output;
do
  echo $output
  usep=$(echo $output | awk '{ print $1}' | cut -d'%' -f1  )
  partition=$(echo $output | awk '{ print $2 }' )
  if [ $usep -ge 90 ]; then
    echo "Running out of space \"$partition ($usep%)\" on $(hostname) as on $(date)" |
     mail -s "Alert: Almost out of disk space $usep%" DataServicesNotification@McKesson.com
  fi
done

#disk_space_home.sh
#!/bin/sh
# disk_space_home.sh
# Will check if /home directory is over 90% on prod servers outside of dsgrid02a
# B.Oliver 7-22-22

df -H | grep -vE '^Filesystem|tmpfs|cdrom' | awk '{ print $5 " " $6 }' | while read output;
do
  echo $output
  usep=$(echo $output | awk '{ print $1}' | cut -d'%' -f1  )
  partition=$(echo $output | awk '{ print $2 }' )
  if [ $usep -ge 90 ] && [  $partition == "/home" ]; then
    echo "Running out of space \"$partition ($usep%)\" on $(hostname) as on $(date)" |
     mail -s "Alert: Almost out of disk space $usep%" DataServicesNotification@McKesson.com
  fi
done


#drop_al_index
#!/usr/bin/perl

# al_index_manager: Audit Log Index Manager
# This is a command-line interface to the BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr modules
#
# Author: jmh
#
# Version history:
# 1/10/2006 - Initial release
# 6/4/2007  - Added completion email capability
# 2/2/2016  - Added 'prune_al_index' capability to clean down indexes by retention period 

use warnings;
use strict;

use Data::Dumper;
use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use Mail::SendEasy;

our $VERSION = '1.1';
our $TEMP_DIR = $ENV{TMPDIR};	# temp files for building indexes will go here

our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
our $SMTP_SERVER = $ENV{DEFAULT_SMTP_SERVER};

die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

initialize_logging(logfile => "$DS_BASE_DIR/common/log/al_index_mgr.$$.log", screen_only => 0, screen_threshold => 'ERROR', file_threshold => 'ERROR');

my %params_date_spec_required = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Mandatory range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 0
	}
);

my %params_date_spec_optional = (
	process_date => {
		description => "Optional range or comma-seperated list of process_dates (e.g. YYYYMMDD,YYYYMMDD or YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD)",
		type => SCALAR,
		optional => 1
	}
);

my %params_index_spec_required = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 0 } );
my %params_index_spec_optional = ( index_id => { description => 'Comma-seperated list of unique index_ids', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );
my %params_connection_var = ( connection_var => { description => 'Name of environment variable for database connection', type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_agg_buckets_optional = ( agg_buckets => { description => 'Number of work units to spread aggregation phase over (e.g. 10, 20, 35, etc)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '35' } );

#my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for parse phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );
