#my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx' } );
my %params_agg_host_spec = ( parallel_agg_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec for INSERT phase (e.g. 'rx', 'ds01:2', 'ds02:2,ds03:3,ds04', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_build_priority_spec = ( build_priority => { description => "CPU scheduling priority (nice value from 0 to 19)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => '19' } );

#my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1, default => 'rx:2' } );
my %params_limited_host_spec = ( parallel_hosts => { description => "Host list/group spec (e.g. 'rx', 'rx:2', 'rx3:2,rx6:3,rx7', etc.)", type => SCALAR, optional => 1 } );

my %params_index_profile_attributes = (
                description         =>  { description => 'Description of index (duh)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                field_id            =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP field id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                segment_id          =>  { description => 'Unique parser/NCPDP segment id', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_function  =>  { description => 'Name of BLUELITE::Normalize function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                normalize_params    =>  { description => 'Parameters for normalize_function', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                valid_only_ind      =>  { description => "Set to 1 to limit indexing to 'valid' values when using normalize_function", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                hash_method         =>  { description => "Name of BLUELITE::Normalize hash_method to apply (e.g. 'crc16')", type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_begin  =>  { description => 'First process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1},
                process_date_end    =>  { description => 'Last process date for index (YYYYMMDD)', type => SCALAR, optional => 1}
);

our $script_name = $0;
$script_name =~ s|.*/||g;	# get basename

our $command_meta = {

	build_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index (unconditional)',

		param_validation => {
			%params_date_spec_required,
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&build_al_index
	},

	create_al_index => {
		description => 'Define profile for new index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&create_al_index
	},

	drop_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove all index data and profile',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&drop_al_index
	},

	enable_al_index => {
		description => 'Build index only on process dates not yet enabled',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_optional,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_host_spec,
			%params_agg_host_spec,
			%params_agg_buckets_optional,
			%params_build_priority_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&enable_al_index
	},

	remove_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove index data',	

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&remove_al_index
	},
	
	update_al_index => {
		description => 'Update profile for existing index',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_index_profile_attributes,
			%params_limited_host_spec,
			%params_connection_var
		},

		method => \&update_al_index
	},
	
	prune_al_index => {
		description => 'Remove expired process dates for existing indexes',

		param_validation => {
			%params_index_spec_required,
			%params_date_spec_optional,
		},

		method => \&prune_al_index
	},
};


sub general_usage() {

	print "$script_name version $VERSION\n";
	print "Usage:                         $script_name -email addresses -command -command_parameters\n";
	print "Alternate (equivalent) usage:  command -command_parameters\n\n";
	print "Supported commands are:\n\n";

	foreach my $command (keys %{$command_meta}) {
		print "$command	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{description} . "\n";
	}

	print "\nTo get command-specific help use '$script_name -command -help'  or  'command -help'\n";
}

sub command_usage($) {
  my $command = shift;

	print "Usage: $command -parameters\n";
	print "\nRequired parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && (! $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "\nOptional parameters:\n";

	foreach my $option (keys %{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}}) {
		if ((! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})) ||
			(exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional}) && $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{optional})
		) {
			print "	-$option";

			if (exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description})) {
				print "	" . $command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}->{$option}->{description};
			}

			print "\n";
		}
	}

	print "	-email	Comma-seperated list of email addresses to send to upon completion\n";
}


my $command;

if (! exists($command_meta->{$script_name})) {
	$command = lc(shift @ARGV);
	$command =~ s/^--?//;

	if (($command =~ /^-?-?help/i) or ($command eq '')) {
		general_usage;
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! exists($command_meta->{$command})) {
		die "ERROR: Command '$command' is not supported by the index manager\n";
	}
} else {
	$command = $script_name;
}

if (! exists($command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation})) {
	die "ERROR: Command '$command' has no 'param_validation' info in source code!\n";
}

if ((! defined($ARGV[0])) or ($ARGV[0] =~ /^-?-?help/i)) {
	command_usage($command);
	exit(1);
}

my %option = validate_with (
	params  => \@ARGV,
	spec    => {
							%{$command_meta->{$command}->{param_validation}},
							email => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 }
							},
	called  => $command,
	normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^--?//; return uc $k }
);


our @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS = ();
if (exists($option{CONNECTION_VAR})) {
	push(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS, connection_var => $option{CONNECTION_VAR});
	delete $option{CONNECTION_VAR};
}

#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;

our $index_mgr = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr->new(@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

if (! defined($index_mgr)) {
	die "ERROR: Unable to get new object from BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr\n";
}

##############################################

sub create_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->new_index_profile(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create new index profile object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($index_profile->save_index_profile));

	return 1;
}


sub prune_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  
	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, uc($option->{INDEX_ID}))) {
				
    my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);
    
	  if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
	  	die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object for index : '$index_id'\n";
	  }
		
	  return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));
	  print "\n";
	}
	
	return 1;
}


sub update_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
  my $parallel_hosts;

  my $index_profile = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($index_profile)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not load existing index profile object\n";
	}

	if (defined($option{PARALLEL_HOSTS})) {
		$parallel_hosts = $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
		delete $option{PARALLEL_HOSTS};
	}

	$index_profile->save_index_profile(%{$option});

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(index_id => $option->{INDEX_ID}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (defined($parallel_hosts)) {
		$maint_grp->parallel_hosts($parallel_hosts);
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->prune_index_data));

	return 1;
}


sub index_ids_to_objects($) {
  my $index_ids = shift;
  my %index_list;

	foreach my $index_id (split(/[,\s]+/, $index_ids)) {

		$index_list{$index_id} = $index_mgr->load_index_profile($index_id, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

		if (! defined($index_list{$index_id})) {
			die "ERROR: Could not obtain index object for index_id '$index_id'\n";
		}

	}

	return %index_list;
}


sub convert_process_dates($) {
  my $options = shift;
  my (%process_dates);

	if (defined($options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
		foreach my $element (split(/[,\s]+/, $options->{PROCESS_DATE})) {
			if ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				$process_dates{$1} = 1;

			} elsif ($element =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*-\s*(\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d)\s*$/) {

				if (! exists($options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN})) {
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN} = $1;
					$options->{PROCESS_DATE_END} = $2;
				} else {
					die "ERROR: Currently, only 1 process date range may be specified\n";
				}

			} else {
				die "ERROR: process date spec of '$element' is not valid\n";
			}
		}

		if (scalar(keys %process_dates) >= 1) {
			@{$options->{PROCESS_DATES}} = (sort keys %process_dates);
		}

		delete $options->{PROCESS_DATE};
	}

	return $options;
}


sub build_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->rebuild));

	return 1;
}


sub enable_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, temp_dir => $TEMP_DIR, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	# get a list of all defined indexes if none specified on command line

	if (! exists($option->{INDEX_ID})) {
		foreach my $index_id ($index_mgr->all_indexes) {
			$maint_grp->add_index($index_id);
		}
	}

	return undef if (! defined($maint_grp->enable));

	return 1;
}


sub remove_al_index($) {
  my $option = convert_process_dates(shift);

  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	return $maint_grp->delete;
}


sub drop_al_index($) {
  my $option = shift;
	my %indexes = index_ids_to_objects($option->{INDEX_ID});
  my $undeleted_profiles = 0;
#print "HEY\n";
#print Dumper \@CONNECT_VAR_OPTS;
  my $maint_grp = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::Index_Mgr::Maint_Group->new(%{$option}, @CONNECT_VAR_OPTS);

	if (! defined($maint_grp)) {
		die "ERROR: Could not create Maint_Group object\n";
	}

	if (! $maint_grp->delete) {
		return undef;
	}

	foreach my $index_id (keys %indexes) {

		if (! $indexes{$index_id}->delete_index_profile) {

			print STDERR "ERROR: All index data deleted for index '$index_id', but unable to remove it's index profile definition from database\n";
			$undeleted_profiles++;
		}
	}

	if ($undeleted_profiles) {
		return undef;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}


sub email(@) {

  my $mail = new Mail::SendEasy( smtp => $SMTP_SERVER);

  if (! defined($mail) ) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to establish a SMTP connection to $SMTP_SERVER\n";
    return undef;
  }

  my $status = $mail->send(
    from => 'data.services@relayhealth.com',
    from_title => 'RelayHealth Data Services',
    @_
  );

  if (! $status) {
    print STDERR "ERROR: Failed to be send email\n";
    return undef;
  }

  return 1;
}


##############################################

my ($exit_status, $email);

if (defined($option{EMAIL})) {
	$email = $option{EMAIL};
	delete $option{EMAIL};
}

if ((exists($command_meta->{$command}->{method})) && (exists(&{$command_meta->{$command}->{method}}))) {
	my $ret;

	eval { $ret = $command_meta->{$command}->{method}(\%option) };

	warn $@ if $@;

  my $completion_status;

	if (! defined($ret)) {
		$exit_status = 1;
		$completion_status = 'failed';
	} else {
		$exit_status = 0;
		$completion_status = 'succeeded';
	}

	if (defined($email)) {

		my $option_list = Dumper(\%option);
		$option_list =~ s/\$VAR1/options/;

		email(
			to => $email,
			subject => "$command process $completion_status",
			msg => "The following $command process ${completion_status}:\n\n$option_list\n" . join("\n", $@) . "\n"
		);
	}

	exit($exit_status);
} else {
	die "ERROR: Interface for '$command' not yet supported\n";
}



#dr_validate_config.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
#
#	read in DataRights configuration file, test validity against *.xsd
#
#	dr_validate_config.pl --help
#
#	Oct 29, 2013 Michael Carey
#		BEGIN
#
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

use strict;
use warnings;
use XML::LibXML;
use File::Spec;
use Getopt::Long;

my $xml_file = '';
my $xsd_file = '';
my $help     = '';
my $result = GetOptions(
						 "xml_file=s" => \$xml_file,
						 "xsd_file=s" => \$xsd_file,
						 "help"       => \$help,
						 );

if ($help) {
	show_help();
	exit(0);
}

# for xml config file, if file is not specified on the command line,
# use the path/name stored in PDC_CONFIG_INFO environment variable
my $xml = '';
if ($xml_file) {

	# we will use file from the command line
	print("using $xml_file for test\n");
	$xml = $xml_file;
	
} else {

	print("xml file not specified on command line\n");

	if ( exists $ENV{PDC_CONFIG_INFO} ) {

		$xml = $ENV{PDC_CONFIG_INFO};
		print("using $ENV{PDC_CONFIG_INFO} from environment variable\n");

	} else {

		show_help();
		print("no xml file to validate\n");
		die("PDC_CONFIG_INFO environment variable not defined\n");

	}

} ## end else [ if ($xml_file) ]

# test file for existence and readability, die if bad
test_file($xml);

# if *.xsd file is specified on command line, use that, else
# use environment variable to construct *.xsd
my $xsd = '';
if ($xsd_file) {

	# we will use xsd file from the command line
	print("using $xsd_file for test\n");
	$xsd = $xsd_file;
	
} else {

	print("xsd file not specified on command line\n");

	if ( exists $ENV{PDC_CONFIG_INFO} ) {

		$xsd = $ENV{PDC_CONFIG_INFO};
		print("constructing xsd path/filename from environment variable\n");

	} else {

		show_help();
		print("cannot construct xsd filename, specify one on the cmd line\n");
		die("PDC_CONFIG_INFO environment variable not defined\n");

	}

	# construct *.xsd path/filename
	my $volume;
	my $dirs;
	( $volume, $dirs, $xsd ) = File::Spec->splitpath($xsd);

	# make sure the config file has an xml extension
	if ( $xsd =~ m/.xml$/ ) {

		# good, the config file has an xml extension
	} else {

		print("$xsd does not appear to have an xml extension\n");
		die("cannot construct *.xsd file, provide one on the command line");

	}

	$xsd =~ tr/.xml$/.xsd/;

	$xsd = File::Spec->catpath( $volume, $dirs, $xsd );
	print("using $xsd as template\n");

} ## end else [ if ($xsd_file) ]

# test file for existence and readability, die if bad
test_file($xsd);

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
# open file read in xml config perform some validation
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

my $xml_parser;
my $xml_doc;
my $xmlref;
my $xml_schema;
my $xml_vstat = 1;    # ->validate either returns 0 or dies
eval {
	# validating with XML::LibXML
	$xml_parser = XML::LibXML->new();
	$xml_doc    = $xml_parser->parse_file($xml);
	$xml_schema = XML::LibXML::Schema->new( location => $xsd );
	$xml_vstat  = $xml_schema->validate($xml_doc);

};
if ( ( $xml_vstat != 0 ) || $@ ) {
	die("$xml NOT VALID, $@\n");
}

if ( $xml_vstat == 0 ) {
	print("$xml PASSED VALIDATION!\n");
}

exit(0);

sub show_help {
	print <<EOT;

Validate a DataRights configuration XML file agianst an XSD.  This is a command
line utility for BLUELITE::DataRights.

Usage:

  dr_validate_config.pl --xml_file=FILE [--xsd_file=FILE] [--help]

Options:

  --xml_file=FILE  DataRights xml config file to test for validity
  
  --xsd_file=FILE  Xsd template to use for validating.  If xsd is not specified
                   here, the file defined by environment variable
                   PDC_CONFIG_INFO will be used.  It's xml exension will be
                   converted to xsd.

  --help           Show this help

EOT

	return (1);
} ## end sub show_help

sub test_file {
	my $tst_file = shift() || '';

	# test file for existence and readability
	# make sure the file exists
	if ( -e $tst_file ) {

		# GOOD, file exists
	} else {

		die("file doesn't exist: $tst_file");

	}

	# make sure the config file is readable
	if ( -r $tst_file ) {

		# GOOD, file is readable
	} else {

		die("file not readable: $tst_file");

	}

	return(1);
} ## end sub test_file

=head1 dr_validate_config.pl

Validate a DataRights configuration XML file agianst an XSD.  This is a command
line utility for BLUELITE::DataRights.

=head1 SYNOPSIS

 dr_validate_config.pl  (test config file specified in env var PDC_CONFIG_INFO)
 
 dr_validate_config.pl --xml_file=test_config.xml   (test specified XML file 
                                                     using production XSD.)

 dr_validate_config.pl --xsd_file=test_xsd.xsd  (test production XML file using
                                                 specified XSD)

 dr_validate_config.pl --xml_file=test_config.xml --xsd_file=test_xsd.xsd
                       (test specified XML file using specified XSD file)

 dr_validate_config.pl --help (show help)

 
=head1 DESCRIPTION

This command line utility uses XML::LibXML to test an XML file against an XSD.
If file path/names are not specified on the command line, the environment
variable PDC_CONFIG_INFO is used.

=head2 Options

=over 4

=item --xml_file=FILE

Specify the XML file to test.  If omitted, the environment variable
 PDC_CONFIG_INFO will be used.
 
=item --xsd_file=FILE

Specify the XSD file to use for validation.  If one is not specified, the
environment variable PDC_CONFIG_INFO is used.  The 'xml' extension is replaced
with 'xsd'.

=item --help

Show help text

=back

=head1 AUTHOR

=over 4

=item Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>

=back

=head1 COPYRIGHT

 Copyright 2013 RelayHealth/McKesson.  All rights reserved.

=cut

__END__

#ds_encrypt
#!/usr/bin/perl

# ds_encrypt: encrypt a file in-place
#
# Author: jmh, Per-Se Technologies
# Initial release: 2/10/2006
#
# Note: The goal of this encryption utility is NOT performance.  The goal is to SAFELY replace a unencrypted
# input file with an encrypted version of the file with a ".pgp" extension added to the filename.
#
# The input file must be readable via the 'read_file' command if the -verify option is specified.
#
# Currently, the private key for the encryption recipient must be available so that
# decryption verification can be performed if the -verify option is given.
#
# 6/2006 : Initial release
#
# 10/9/2006 : Added "-compress-level #" and "-compress" options. Default of no compression remains.
#
# Version 1.2: 10/10/2019 J Hess
#
# Added support for repeating the -recipient option when multiple recipients are desired.


use strict;
use warnings;
use String::CRC32;	# used here for verifying input and output equivalency
use Getopt::Long;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s|.*/||g;

# defaults

my $keep_original = 0;
my $exit_success = 0;
my $verify = 0;
my @recipient = ();
my $overwrite_output = 0;
my $success_on_skip = 0;
my ($min_file_age, $success_message, $compress_level, $compress);

GetOptions(
						"keep-original" => \$keep_original,
						"exit=s" => \$exit_success,
						"recipient=s" => \@recipient,
						"verify" => \$verify,
						"overwrite" => \$overwrite_output,
						"min-file-age=s" => \$min_file_age,
						"success-on-skip" => \$success_on_skip,
						"success-message=s" => \$success_message,
						"compress-level=s" => \$compress_level,
						"compress" => \$compress
) || exit(1);

if (! @recipient) {
	@recipient = ($ENV{DEFAULT_PGP_RECIPIENT});
}

if (! @recipient) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: -recipient not specified and DEFAULT_PGP_RECIPIENT variable not set\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (! defined($compress_level)) {
	if (defined($compress)) {
		$compress_level = 6;
	} else {
		$compress_level = 0;
	}
}

my $fname = shift(@ARGV);

if ( (! defined($fname)) or (! (length($fname) >= 1)) ) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: encrypt a file in-place, with extremely thorough error checking\n";
	print STDERR "Usage: $PGM [-keep-original] [-verify] [-exit exit_code] [-recipient key_id] [-min-file-age #_seconds] [-success-on-skip] [-compress] [-compress-level #] file [destination_dir]\n";
	print STDERR "-recipient may be repeated for multiple recipients\n";
	print STDERR "-compress-level # can be from 0 (no compression) to 9 (most compression) . Default is 0.\n";
	print STDERR "-compress implies compression level of 6 .\n";
	exit(1);
}


# sanity check input/output filenames

if (! -f $fname) {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: '$fname' does not exist\n";
}

if ($fname =~ /[.](pgp)|(gpg)$/i) {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: The file '$fname' is already encrypted\n";
}

if (defined($min_file_age) && ($min_file_age > 0)) {
	my ($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$fsize,$atime,$mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($fname);

	if ($mtime > (time - $min_file_age)) {

		if ($success_on_skip) {
			exit($exit_success);
		} else {
			die "ERROR: $PGM: The file '$fname' has been modified within the last $min_file_age seconds, and the '-success-on-skip' option was NOT specified\n";
		}

	}
}

#

my $output_file;
my $destination = shift(@ARGV);

if (defined($destination)) {

	if ((-d $destination) || (-l $destination)) {
		my $fname_base = $fname;
		$fname_base =~ s|.*/||g;

		$output_file = "${destination}/${fname_base}.pgp";
	} else {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: Optional 2nd parameter is not a directory or symbolic link. Only 1 file can be encrypted.\n";
	}

} else {
	$output_file = "${fname}.pgp";
}

if ($fname eq $output_file) {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: Output file name derived to same as input file name of '$output_file'\n";
}


if ($#ARGV >= 0) {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: Too many arguments\n";
}

my $original_crc;

if ($verify) {
	# get checksum of original file so we can compare to output checksum later

	open(ORIG, "read_file $fname |") || die "ERROR: $PGM: Cannot read contents of $fname to get checksum\n";
	$original_crc = crc32(*ORIG);
	close(ORIG);

	if ($? != 0) {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: could not read '$fname' via read_file\n";
	}

	if ((! defined($original_crc)) or (! (length($original_crc) >= 1)) ) {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: Unable to get valid checksum for input file $fname\n";
	}
}


if ($overwrite_output && (-f $output_file) ) {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: Output file $output_file already exists, and --overwrite option not specified!\n";
}

my $recipient_args = join(' ', map { "--recipient '$_'" } @recipient);
my $encrypt_command = qq/gpg --no-permission-warning --no-random-seed-file --batch --yes --quiet --no-tty $recipient_args -z $compress_level --encrypt --output $output_file $fname/;

#print $encrypt_command . "\n";

# perform encryption

my $ret = system($encrypt_command);
$ret = $ret >> 8;

if ($ret != 0) {

	# get rid of encrypted output file since it's no good

	if (-f $fname) {	# just to be safe :-)
		unlink($output_file);
	}

	die "ERROR: $PGM: Problem encrypting input file '$fname' to output file '$output_file'\n";
}


if ($verify) {
	# get checksum of encrypted file (after decrypting and uncompressing via read_file) so we can compare to earlier input checksum

	open(NEW, "read_file $output_file |") || die "ERROR: $PGM: Cannot read contents of $output_file to get checksum\n";
	my $new_crc = crc32(*NEW);
	close(NEW);

	if ($? != 0) {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: could not read '$output_file' via read_file\n";
	}

	if ((! defined($new_crc)) or (! (length($new_crc) >= 1)) ) {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: Unable to get valid checksum for output file $output_file\n";
	}

	# verify that contents of input is equivalent to output via checksum values

	if ($original_crc ne $new_crc) {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: Validation of input file $fname with output file $output_file failed!\n";
	}
}

# set mod times and perms of outfile to same as inputfile

$ret = system(qq/touch -r $fname $output_file/);
$ret = $ret >> 8;

if ($ret != 0) {
	print STDERR "Warning: $PGM: Unable to reset permissions and modification times of output file $output_file\n";
}


# use gpg program to verify output file is really a valid encrypted file

$ret = system(qq/gpg --no-permission-warning --quiet --no-tty --verify-files $output_file/);
$ret = $ret >> 8;

if ($ret != 0) {

	# get rid of encrypted output file since it's no good

	if (-f $fname) {	# just to be safe :-)
		unlink($output_file);
	}

	die "ERROR: $PGM: Ouput file '$output_file' is not a valid encrypted file\n";
}



# Encryption worked. File comparison checked out OK. GPG integrity verification passed.
# So now we can safely remove the original input file and exit with a successful status
# (unless SOMEHOW input and output files do not still exist, which would be really weird).

if (-f $fname) {
	if (-f $output_file) {
		if (! $keep_original) {
			if (! unlink($fname)) {
				die "ERROR: $PGM: Unable to delete the input file $fname after encrypting to $output_file\n";
			}
		}
	} else {
		die "ERROR: $PGM: Output file $output_file mysteriously disappeared after encrypting from $fname\n";
	}
} else {
	die "ERROR: $PGM: Input file $fname mysteriously disappeared after encrypting to $output_file\n";
}

if (defined($success_message)) {
	print STDERR $success_message . "\n";
}

exit($exit_success);


#dump_txn
#!/usr/bin/perl

# dump_txn: Show entire parsed NCPDP txns in human-readable format, based on various search criteria
# Author: J Hess, RelayHealth, 2010
#
# Version history:
# v1.0: Initial release
#
# v1.1: The '-pdc' criteria will now use the pharmacy filter/index when possible
#
# v1.2:
# Added the following filters to the command line:
#  -next-bin           {from tail_next_bin_code}
#  -b2                 {svc provider qualifier}
#  -exclude-ppe-batch  {Omnicare data capture txns}
#  -pcn
#  -pid                {source pid}
#
# Changed hop filter name internally from 'PPE' to 'HOP' (new alias in NCPDP parser).
#
# Changed the way script name is recognized for run mode of txn vs. transmission dump.
#
# v1.3:
# Added the following filters to the command line:
#  -resp               {txn response status}
#
# v1.4 5/11/2011:
#
# 1) Added the following command-line options:
# -sort
# -exclude-seg
# -seg-fields
# -format
# -log-level
#
# 2) Changed the default parser logging level to ERROR (instead of parser default of INFO)
#
#
# v1.6 2/19/2013
#
# 1) Added "raw" format to -format option, which yields raw request/response with a timestamp prefix
#
# v1.7 1/29/2014
#
# 1) Added -exclude-test command-line option
#
# v1.9 9/15/2014
# 1) Remove include_test and replace with include_pids (including all currently known)
#
# v1.95 12/10/2014
# 1) Change include_pids to 'ALL'
#

my $time0 = time;

use warnings;
use strict;

use BLUELITE::NCPDP::Parser;
use Getopt::Long;
use Data::Dumper;
use BLUELITE::Dimension::PharmacyGroup;
use BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::File;
use BLUELITE::Dimension::Contractual;
use BLUELITE::Logger;

my $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/^.*\///g;

sub get_pharmacy_info($) {
  my $pdc = shift;
	my $info = { use_filter => 'N' };

	die "PDC is empty!\n" if ($pdc =~ /^\s*$/);

	if ($pdc !~ /^\s*(ALL|12)\s*$/i) {
		my @stores = ();
		my $use_filter = 'N';

		my $search_result = BLUELITE::Dimension::Contractual->search( product_code => $pdc, latest_date => 1, status => 'N');

		foreach my $row (@{$search_result}) {
			if (($row->customer_type eq 'N') || ($row->customer_type eq 'P')) {
				push(@stores, $row->customer_num);
				$use_filter = 'Y';
			} else {
				print STDERR "Warning: Cannot use pharmacy filter/index with PDC '$pdc' due to inclusion of customer_type '" . $row->customer_type . "'\n";
				@stores = ();
				$use_filter = 'N';
				last;
			}
		}

		$info = { use_filter => $use_filter, values => \@stores };
	}

	if ($pdc =~ /^\s*12\s*$/) {
		print STDERR "Warning: Cannot use pharmacy filter/index with PDC '$pdc' because that is a 'as was' PDC\n";
	}

	return $info;
}


my (@pharmacies, @rx, @post_dates, @dos, @txn_id, @auditlog, @prescriber, @ndc, @bin, @next_bin, $hop, @b1, @b2, @script, @cps_group, @pcn, @pid, $pharmacy_fname, @fill, @resp, @txn_type);

my $pdc = 'ALL';
my $exclude_verboten = 0;
my $exclude_troop = 0;
my $exclude_ppe_batch = 0;
my $sort = 0;
my @seg_fields = ();
my @exclude_seg = ();
my $log_level = 'ERROR';
my $format = 'full';

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
        print "Usage: $PGM -post-date YYYYMMDD|YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD [-options]\n";
				print "  options:\n";
				print join('   ',
					"     [-txn-id t]                    {t is Data Svcs txn id}\n",
					"  [-script rxnum=#,pharmacy=#]   {may use NPI or NABP}\n",
					"  [-pharmacy-id #]               {may use NPI or NABP}\n",
					"  [-pharmacy-file fname]         {may use NPI or NABP}\n",
					"  [-cps-group g]                 {latest stores in CPS group g}\n",
					"  [-rx #]\n",
					"* [-fill #]\n",
					"  [-b1 #]                        {raw Service Provider ID}\n",
					"* [-b2 #]                        {Service Provider ID qualifier}\n",
					"* [-dos YYYYMMDD]\n",
					"  [-prescriber p]\n",
					"  [-ndc n]\n",
					"  [-bin b]\n",
					"* [-next-bin b]\n",
					"* [-pcn p]\n",
					"* [-pid p]\n",
					"* [-resp r]\n",
					"* [-hop filo|payer|lifo|ppe]\n",
					"  [-auditlog fname]\n",
					"  [-pdc p]\n",
					"* [-txn-type billing|reversals|rebill]\n",
					"* [-exclude-verboten]\n",
					"* [-exclude-troop]\n",
					"* [-exclude-ppe-batch]\n",
					"  [-sort]\n",
					"  [-seg-fields field:seg]\n",
					"  [-exclude-seg seg]\n",
					"  [-log-level INFO|WARN|ERROR]\n",
					"  [-format f]                     {f=basic, full (default), raw}\n"
				) . "\n";

        print "Notes:\n";
				print "1) Most parameters above may be repeated for multiple values (e.g. -ndc 1 -ndc 2 -ndc 3)\n";
				print "2) * These fields are NOT indexed.\n";
				print "3) The -post-date parameter is not required when -txn-id or -auditlog parameter is used\n";
				print "4) Only txns meeting ALL specified criteria will be found (i.e. parameters are ANDed together)\n";
        exit(0);
}

my $ret = GetOptions(
  'pharmacy-id=s@' => \@pharmacies,
  'pharmacy-file=s' => \$pharmacy_fname,
  'rx=s@' => \@rx,
  'post-date=s' => \@post_dates,
  'dos=s@' => \@dos,
  'txn-id=s@' => \@txn_id,
	'auditlog=s@' => \@auditlog,
	'prescriber=s@' => \@prescriber,
	'ndc=s@' => \@ndc,
	'bin=s@' => \@bin,
	'next-bin=s@' => \@next_bin,
	'hop=s' => \$hop,
	'b1=s@' => \@b1,
	'b2=s@' => \@b2,
	'script=s@' => \@script,
	'txn-type=s@' => \@txn_type,
	'exclude-verboten' => \$exclude_verboten,
	'exclude-troop' => \$exclude_troop,
	'exclude-ppe-batch' => \$exclude_ppe_batch,
	'pdc=s' => \$pdc,
	'cps-group=s@' => \@cps_group,
	'pcn=s@' => \@pcn,
	'pid=s@' => \@pid,
	'fill=s@' => \@fill,
	'resp=s@' => \@resp,
	'sort' => \$sort,
	'seg-fields=s@' => \@seg_fields,
	'exclude-seg=s@' => \@exclude_seg,
	'log-level=s' => \$log_level,
	'format=s' => \$format
);

die "Extraneous parameters on command-line: " . join(' ', @ARGV) . "\n" if (@ARGV);

if ((@txn_id || @auditlog) && (! @post_dates)) {
	my (%pd, $post_date);

	my $al_file = BLUELITE::TandemSwitchAuditLog::File->new;

	foreach my $txn_id (@txn_id) {
		$post_date = $al_file->process_date(rx_txn_id => $txn_id);
		die "Cannot get post_date for txn-id $txn_id\n" if (! defined($post_date));
		$pd{$post_date} = undef
	}

	foreach my $al (@auditlog) {
		$post_date = $al_file->process_date(auditlog_name => $al);
		$pd{$post_date} = undef;
	}

	@post_dates = (keys %pd);
}

sub scrub($) {
  my $value = shift;

	if (defined($value)) {
		$value =~ s/^\s+//;
		$value =~ s/\s+$//;
		$value = uc($value);
	}

	return $value;
}

my $sf_opt;

$format = lc($format);

if (defined($format) && $format eq 'basic') {
	if (@exclude_seg || @seg_fields) {
		die "Cannot use -format basic option together with -seg-fields or -exclude-seg options\n";
	}

	@exclude_seg = ('US');
	@seg_fields = qw(REQ_P_ARRIVAL_TIME:UQ TRANSACTION_ID:UG PHARM_NPI:UT PHARM_NABP:UT);
}

if (@exclude_seg) {

	foreach my $segment (@exclude_seg) {
		my $seg = scrub($segment);
		$sf_opt->{$seg} = [];
	}
}

if (@seg_fields) {
	foreach my $seg_fld (@seg_fields) {
		my ($field, $seg) = split(':', $seg_fld);
		$seg = scrub($seg);
		$field = scrub($field);

		push(@{$sf_opt->{$seg}}, $field);
	}
}

my @dump_opts = ();
@dump_opts = (segment_fields => $sf_opt) if (defined($sf_opt));

initialize_logging(screen_threshold => $log_level, screen_only => 1);

my $parser = BLUELITE::NCPDP::Parser->new;
$parser->source_parser_config(include_ndc_prefix => 0, include_ndc_tail_info => 0);

my @filter_opts = (index_required => 1);
my $include_verboten = $exclude_verboten ? 0 : 1;
my $include_troop = $exclude_troop ? 0 : 1;
my $include_ppe_batch = $exclude_ppe_batch ? 0 : 1;

# Add desired filters 

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'CONTRACT', include => $pdc, include_verboten => $include_verboten, include_troop => $include_troop, include_ppe_batch => $include_ppe_batch, include_pids => ['ALL']);
my $pharmacy_info = get_pharmacy_info($pdc);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'PHARMACY', values => $pharmacy_info->{values}) if ($pharmacy_info->{use_filter} =~ /Y/i);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'PHARMACY', values_file => $pharmacy_fname) if (defined($pharmacy_fname));

die "The -post-date parameter is required\n" if (! @post_dates);

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'PROCESS_DATE', values => \@post_dates) if (scalar(@post_dates) >= 1);

die "Cannot use both -cps-group and -pharmacy-id parameters together\n" if (@cps_group && @pharmacies);

if (@cps_group) {
	my $pharm_group = BLUELITE::Dimension::PharmacyGroup->new || die "Cannot obtain BLUELITE::Dimension::Pharmacy_Group object : $@\n";

	foreach my $group (@cps_group) {
		my $result = $pharm_group->search(latest_date => 1, group_id => $group, latest_date => 1);

		foreach my $row (@{$result}) {
			push(@pharmacies, $row->{ATTRIBUTE}->{npi}) if (defined($row->{ATTRIBUTE}->{npi}));
			push(@pharmacies, $row->{ATTRIBUTE}->{nabp}) if (defined($row->{ATTRIBUTE}->{nabp}));
		}
	}

	die "No pharmacies in requested CPS group codes\n" if (! @pharmacies);
}

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'PHARMACY', values => \@pharmacies, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@pharmacies) >= 1);

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'RX', values => \@rx, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@rx) >= 1);

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'TRANSACTION_ID', values => \@txn_id) if (scalar(@txn_id) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'AUDITLOG', values => \@auditlog) if (scalar(@auditlog) >= 1);

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'PRID', values => \@prescriber, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@prescriber) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NDC', values => \@ndc, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@ndc) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'BIN', values => \@bin, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@bin) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'TAIL_NEXT_BIN_CODE', segment_id => 'UQ', values => \@next_bin) if (scalar(@next_bin) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'HOP', values => [$hop]) if (defined($hop));
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'B1', segment_id => 'RQ', values => \@b1, @filter_opts) if (scalar(@b1) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'D1', segment_id => 'RQ', values => \@dos) if (scalar(@dos) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'A4', segment_id => 'RQ', values => \@pcn) if (scalar(@pcn) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'ITB_SID', segment_id => 'UT', values => \@pid) if (scalar(@pid) >= 1);
$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'NCPDP_FIELD', field_id => 'AN', segment_id => '21', values => \@resp) if (scalar(@resp) >= 1);

my $tstmp_format = DateTime::Format::Strptime->new( pattern => '%Y%m%d%H%M%S%3N');

my @scripts = ();

if (@script) {
	foreach my $script (@script) {
		my @params = split(/\s*,\s*/, $script);

		die "-script param '$script' must contain exactly 2 name/value pairs seperated by comma\n" if (scalar(@params) != 2);

		my ($rx, $phm, $name, $value);

		foreach my $param (@params) {
			if ($param =~ /^\s*(\w+)\s*=\s*(\w+)\s*$/) {
				($name, $value) = ($1, $2);
			} else {
				die "-script param '$script' contains param '$param', which is not a valid 'name=value' assignment\n";
			}

			if ($name =~ /^rx/i) {
				$rx = $value;
			} elsif ($name =~ /^(ph|nabp|npi)/i) {
				$phm = $value;
			} else {
				die "-script param '$script' contains invalid name of '$name'\n";
			}
		}

		die "-script param '$script' does not contain 'rx=####' name/value pair\n" if (! defined($rx));
		die "-script param '$script' does not contain 'pharmacy=####' name/value pair\n" if (! defined($phm));

		push(@scripts, { phm => $phm, rxnum => $rx });
	}

	$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'SCRIPT', values => \@scripts);
}

$parser->add_NCPDP_filter(name => 'TRANS_TYPE', values => \@txn_type) if (@txn_type);

my $pt;
my $txn = 0;

my $script = $0;
$script =~ s/.*\///g;

my $dump_txn;

if ($PGM =~ /mission/i) {
	$dump_txn = 0;
} else {
	$dump_txn = 1;
}

my %xmissions = ();
my $num_xmissions = 0;
my @txns = ();

TXN:

while ($pt = $parser->parse_next_transaction()) {

	if (scalar(@b2) >= 1) {
		my $b2 = $pt->get_value(field_id => 'B2', segment_id => 'RQ');
		my $found_matching_b2 = 0;

		B2:
		foreach my $search_b2 (@b2) {
			if (
					(($search_b2 =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) && ($b2 =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) && ($search_b2 == $b2)) ||
					($search_b2 eq $b2)
					) {
				$found_matching_b2 = 1;
				last B2;	# at least one B2 we're searching for matches
			}
		}

		next TXN if (! $found_matching_b2);
	}

	if (scalar(@fill) >= 1) {
		my $fill_num = $pt->get_value(field_id => 'D3');
		my $found_matching_fill = 0;

		FILL:
		foreach my $search_fill (@fill) {
			if (
					(($search_fill =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) && ($fill_num =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) && ($search_fill == $fill_num)) ||
					($search_fill eq $fill_num)
					) {
				$found_matching_fill = 1;
				last FILL;	# at least one fill # we're searching for matches
			}
		}

		next TXN if (! $found_matching_fill);
	}

	if ($dump_txn) {

		if ($sort) {
			push(@txns, { xmission => $pt, group => $pt->current_group, time => $pt->get_value(field_id => 'REQ_P_ARRIVAL_TIME', segment_id => 'UQ') });
		} else {
			if ($format !~ /raw/i) {
				$pt->dump_transaction(@dump_opts);
			} else {
				my $tstamp = $pt->get_value(field_id => 'REQ_P_ARRIVAL_TIME', segment_id => 'UQ');
				$tstamp->set_formatter($tstmp_format);
				print $tstamp . '-' . $pt->source_transmission->request() . chr(0x1f) . $pt->source_transmission->response();
			}
		}

	} else {
		my $xmission_id = $pt->get_value(field_id => 'TRANSMISSION_ID');

		if (! exists($xmissions{$xmission_id})) {
			print "Group " . $pt->current_group . " below is one of the matching txns\n";

			$pt->dump_transmission(@dump_opts);
			$xmissions{$xmission_id} = undef;
			$num_xmissions++;
		}
	}

	$txn++;

	print "\n\n" if (! $sort);
}

my $elapsed = time - $time0;

if ($dump_txn) {
	my $sort_message = '';

	if ($sort) {

		foreach my $txn (sort { $a->{time} <=> $b->{time} } @txns) {
			if ($format !~ /raw/i) {
				$txn->{xmission}->dump_transaction(group => $txn->{group}, @dump_opts);
			} else {
				my $tstamp = $txn->{xmission}->get_value(field_id => 'REQ_P_ARRIVAL_TIME', segment_id => 'UQ');
				$tstamp->set_formatter($tstmp_format);
				print $tstamp . '-' . $txn->{xmission}->source_transmission->request() . chr(0x1f) . $txn->{xmission}->source_transmission->response();
			}
			print "\n\n";
		}

		$sort_message = 'sorted';
	}

	print "Dumped $txn matching $sort_message txns in $elapsed seconds\n";
} else {
	print "Dumped $num_xmissions transmissions containing $txn matching txns in $elapsed seconds\n";
}



#elig_start
#!/usr/bin/bash

#Author: W Hampton
export USER=`whoami`
if [ "${USER}" = "webadmin" ];
then
  # Find current PIDs running Glassfish
  export GLASS_PID_PATIENT=`ps ux | grep -w "patient" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
  export GLASS_PID_PATIENTRX=`ps ux | grep -w "patientrx" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
  export GLASS_PID_ADDRESS=`ps ux | grep -w "correctAddress1" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
  # Checking if the PIDs are running
  if [ "${GLASS_PID_ADDRESS}" = "" ];
  then
     echo "Starting domain=[correctAddress]...."
     /dsapp/prod/shared/ca/correctAddress/bin/ca_restart.sh
	   
  else

     echo "domain=[correctAddress] running: ${GLASS_PID_ADDRESS}"
  fi
    # Checking for patient PIDs
    if [ "${GLASS_PID_PATIENT}" = "" ];
     then
        echo "Starting domain=[patient]..."
	/dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/gf/current/bin/asadmin start-domain patient
	      
    else
        echo "domain=[patient] running: ${GLASS_PID_PATIENT}"
  fi
        # Checking for patientrx PIDs
        if [ "${GLASS_PID_PATIENTRX}" = "" ];
     then
        echo "Starting domain=[patientrx]..."
	/dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/gf/current/bin/asadmin start-domain patientrx
	      

    else
        echo "domain=[patientrx] running: ${GLASS_PID_PATIENTRX}"
  fi

else
    echo "Need to be webadmin to execute."
fi

  export GLASS_PID_PATIENTRX=`ps ux | grep -w "patientrx" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`

        # Checking for correctAddress1 PIDs

    export TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR=`ps ux | grep -w "Dcatalina" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
    #Checking if the PIDs are running
    if [ "${GLASS_PID_PSCBR}" = "" ]
  then
     echo "Starting domain1..."
	  /dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/pscbr/glassfish-3.1.2.2/glassfish/bin/asadmin start-domain domain1
  else
     echo "domain=[domain1] running: ${GLASS_PID_PSCBR}"
   fi
     if [ "${TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR}" = "" ]
     then
        echo "Starting Tomcat..."
	    cd /dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/pscbr/tomcat/current/bin/ && ./start_tomcat
    else
        echo "Tomcat is running: ${TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR}"
    fi
    else
        echo "Need to be pscbr to execute."
fi

    export TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR=`ps ux | grep -w "Dcatalina" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`

#emi_pscbr_stop
#!/usr/bin/bash


#Author: W Hampton
#Stop GlassFish/Tomcat EMI

export USER=`whoami`
if [ "${USER}" = "pscbr" ];
then
    # Find current PIDs running Glassfish
    export GLASS_PID_PSCBR=`ps ux | grep -w "domain" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
    export TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR=`ps ux | grep -w "Dcatalina" | grep -v "grep" | tr -s ' ' | cut -f 2 -d ' '`
    #Checking if the PIDs are running
    if [ "${GLASS_PID_PSCBR}" = "" ]
  then
     echo "domain1 Stopped..."
  else
     echo "Stopping domain1"
	   /dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/pscbr/glassfish-3.1.2.2/glassfish/bin/asadmin stop-domain domain1
	   sleep 6; kill -9 ${GLASS_PID_PSCBR}
   fi
     if [ "${TOMCAT_PID_PSCBR}" = "" ]
     then
        echo "Tomcat is stopped..."
    else
        echo "Stopping Tomcat..."
	     cd /dsapp/prod/local/${HOSTNAME%%.*}/pscbr/tomcat/current/bin/ && ./stop_tomcat
    fi
    else
        echo "Need to be pscbr to execute."
fi

}



#encrypt_files
#!/usr/bin/perl

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
#
# encrypt_files - Submit request to have a file or files encrypted to your
#                 public key for analysis.
#
# 20160928 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
#
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

use strict;
use warnings;
use DateTime;
use IO::File;
use File::Spec;
use File::stat;
use Getopt::Long;
use Term::ReadLine;
use Mail::SendEasy;

# todo: set in common profile during deployment for prod (/ds/env/prod/ENREQ)
# $ENV{ENREQDIR} = '/ds/env/qaqc/ENREQ';

if ( !$ENV{ENREQDIR} ) {
	print "The environment variable ENREQDIR must be set to the root application\n";
	print "directory.  (perhaps /ds/env/prod/ENREQ).\n";
	exit 1;
}

my $help       = '';
my $noconf     = '';
my $opt_result = GetOptions(
	'noconf' => \$noconf,
	'help'   => \$help,
	);

if ($help) {
	show_help();
	exit 0;
}

if ( !@ARGV ) {
	print "ERROR: You must specify files to process\n";
	show_help();
	exit 1;
}

my $qdir     = $ENV{ENREQDIR} . '/common/incoming';
my $udb      = $ENV{ENREQDIR} . '/common/etc/users.txt';
my $ublfile  = $ENV{ENREQDIR} . '/common/etc/user_blist.txt';
my $emblfile = $ENV{ENREQDIR} . '/common/etc/email_blist.txt';
my $user     = getpwuid($>);                                     # get current user name

if ( !$user ) {
	print "ERROR: Could not determine effective user id\n";
	exit 1;
}

# username cannot be from a blacklist
my $fh = IO::File->new( $ublfile, O_RDONLY ) or die("opening $ublfile, $!");
my $usermatch = 0;
while ( my $line = <$fh> ) {
	$line =~ s/\r|\n//g;
	if ( !$line )             { next; }                          # skip blank lines
	if ( $line =~ m/^\s*#+/ ) { next; }                          # skip comments
	if ( $user eq $line ) { $usermatch = 1; }
}
if ( $fh->error() ) { die("reading $ublfile, $!"); }
$fh->close() or die "closing $ublfile, $!";

if ($usermatch) {
	print "ERROR: Current user is prohibited from using this application.\n";
	print "See Data Services.\n";
	exit 1;
}

# look for user in file, get associated email address
my $email = '';
$fh = IO::File->new( $udb, O_RDONLY ) or die("opening $udb, $!");
while ( my $line = <$fh> ) {
	$line =~ s/\r|\n//g;
	if ( !$line )             { next; }    # skip blank lines
	if ( $line =~ m/^\s*#+/ ) { next; }    # skip comments
	my ( $u, $e ) = split( /\|/, $line );
	if ( $user eq $u ) {
		$email = $e;
		last;
	}
}
if ( $fh->error() ) { die("reading $udb, $!"); }
$fh->close() or die "closing $udb, $!";

if ( !$email ) {
	print "ERROR: You are not listed as a user for this application.\n";
	print "See Data Services to be added.\n";
	exit 1;
}

# associated email address cannot be from a blacklist
$fh = IO::File->new( $emblfile, O_RDONLY ) or die("opening $emblfile, $!");
my $emailmatch = 0;
while ( my $line = <$fh> ) {
	$line =~ s/\r|\n//g;
	if ( !$line )             { next; }    # skip blank lines
	if ( $line =~ m/^\s*#+/ ) { next; }    # skip comments
	$line = lc $line;
	if ( $email eq $line ) { $emailmatch = 1; }
}
if ( $fh->error() ) { die("reading $emblfile, $!"); }
$fh->close() or die "closing $emblfile, $!";

if ($emailmatch) {
	print "ERROR: Your associated email address is not allowed for this application.\n";
	print "Your user record has been incorrectly added.  See Data Services.\n";
	exit 1;
}

# validate email address, must be mckesson.com, relayhealth.com
$email = lc $email;
if ( $email !~ m/^([a-zA-Z0-9_\-\.]+)\@(mckesson\.com|relayhealth\.com)$/ ) {
	print "ERROR: Associated email address must be \@mckesson.com, \@relayhealth.com.\n";
	print "Your user record has been incorrectly added.  See Data Services.\n";
	exit 1;
}

# iterate
my %oklist   = ();
my @faillist = ();
foreach my $file (@ARGV) {
	$file =~ s/\r|\n//g;

	# if relative path, prepend working directory
	if ( $file !~ m/^\// ) { $file = $ENV{PWD} . "/$file"; }

	# we don't want duplicates
	if ( exists $oklist{$file} ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'file is a duplicate'} );
		next;
	}

	# must have a .pgp extension
	if ( $file !~ m/\.pgp$/ ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'file has no pgp extension'} );
		next;
	}

	# must be readable
	if ( !-r $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'file is not readable'} );
		next;
	}

	# be a plain file
	if ( !-f $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'file is not a plain file'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be a directory
	if ( -d $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a directory'} );
		next;
	}

	# the file must not itself be a link
	if ( -l $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a link'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be zero length
	if ( -z $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'file is zero length'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be a named pipe
	if ( -p $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a named pipe'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be a socket
	if ( -S $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a socket'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be a block special file
	if ( -b $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a block special file'} );
		next;
	}

	# must not be a character special file
	if ( -c $file ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'this is a character special file'} );
		next;
	}

	# must have group read permission bit set
	my $fstat = stat($file);
	if ( !( $fstat->mode & 0040 ) ) {
		push( @faillist, {file => $file, reason => 'group read permission is not set'} );
		next;
	}

	$oklist{$file} = '';
} ## end foreach my $file (@ARGV)

# display summary of request
foreach my $file ( sort keys %oklist ) {
	print "file: $file\n";
}
if ( scalar @faillist ) {
	foreach my $file ( sort @faillist ) {
		print "skipped: " . $file->{file} . "\n\t=> " . $file->{reason} . "\n";
	}
}

my $numfiles = scalar( keys %oklist );
print "Total number of valid files for submission: $numfiles\n";
if ( $numfiles > 100 ) {
	print "ERROR: You may only submit up to 100 files per request.\n";
	show_help();
	exit 1;
}
if ( $numfiles < 1 ) {
	print "WARNING: No files selected.\n";
	show_help();
	exit 0;
}

# prompt the user to create request
if ( !$noconf ) {
	my $term     = Term::ReadLine->new('Get Answer');
	my $response = '';
	do {
		$response = $term->readline('Submit Request? [y/n]: ');
		$response = lc $response;
	} while ( defined $response && $response !~ m/^y$|^yes$|^no$|^n$/ );
	if ( !defined $response || $response =~ m/^no$|^n$/ ) {
		print "Request cancelled by user.\n";
		exit 0;
	}
} ## end if ( !$noconf )

# formulate request
my $time     = DateTime->now->set_time_zone('America/New_York')->strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S');
my $username = getpwuid($>);
my $reqfname = File::Spec->catfile( $qdir, "$time-$username.txt" );
my $request  = '';
foreach my $file ( sort keys %oklist ) {
	$request .= "$file\n";
}

# write request file
$fh = IO::File->new( $reqfname, O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_EXCL | O_APPEND )
  or die("opening $reqfname, $!");
print $fh $request;
if ( $fh->error() ) { die "reading $reqfname, $!"; }
$fh->close() or die("closing $reqfname, $!");

# send email copy of request to user
my $m = Mail::SendEasy->new( smtp => 'localhost' );
if ( defined $m ) {
	my $s = $m->send(
		from       => 'dataservicesnotification@relayhealth.com',
		from_title => 'Data Services',
		to         => $email,
		subject    => 'Encryption request submitted',
		msg        => $request,
		);
	if ( !$s ) {
		print $m->error . "\n";
		print "Problem encountered while sending email copy of request.\n";
		print "You will not receive a copy of this request via email.\n";
	}
} else {
	print "Could not connect to local SMTP server.\n";
	print "You will not receive a copy of this request via email.\n";
}

print "Request submitted!\n";
exit 0;

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

sub show_help {
	print q{
encrypt_files [-noconf] file1 [file2, *.pgp, 201608*.pgp, ...]

Submit request to have a file or files encrypted to your public key for
analysis.

 -noconf   Do not prompt before submission.
};
	print "\n";
}

#env_date
#!/bin/bash
export DATE=`date +%Y%m%d`
export YMONTH=`date +%Y%m`
export YEAR=`date +%Y`

#eva
#!/usr/bin/perl

#========================================================================
#  
#  
#  Extract Validation and Analysis (EVA)
#  
#  
#  Requires:	Perl 5.001m of greater
#  
#  Version:	1.30
#  
#  Modification History
#  
#  	John Dennis - August 1995
#  
#  	Modified EVA to support fixed-length extract files.  This
#  	required a modification to the configuration file layout.
#  
#  	John Dennis - June 1996
#  
#  	Modified EVA to support UNIX and Windows 95/DOS with only one
#  	version of source code.  This version supports Windows 95
#  	Perl 5.001m or greater.
#  
#  	John Dennis - May 1999
#  
#  	Corrected several bugs within the code
#  
#  Copyright 1994
#  Dennis & Hess
#  
#  
#========================================================================

$Platform = "UNIX";

if ($ENV{"COMSPEC"})
{
	$Platform = "DOS";
}
else
{
	$Platform = "UNIX";
}


use Getopt::Std;
use Text::ParseWords;

format STDOUT =
      @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<< @######  @####.##%
$Format_Value, $Format_Occurences, $Format_Pct
.

$Cutoff = 25;
$Default_Delimiter = "|";
$Debug = 0;
$Check_Primary_Key = "N";
srand;



$Display_Non_Printable_Char[0] = "^@";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[1] = "^A";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[2] = "^B";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[3] = "^C";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[4] = "^D";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[5] = "^E";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[6] = "^F";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[7] = "^G";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[8] = "^H";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[9] = "^I";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[10] = "^J";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[11] = "^K";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[12] = "^L";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[13] = "^M";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[14] = "^N";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[15] = "^O";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[16] = "^P";
$Display_Non_Printable_Char[17] = "^Q";
